Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:3.6

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena upakkamitvā asuciṁ mocentassa saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.2
Pali: Sāvatthiyaṁ paññatto. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.4
Pali: Āyasmantaṁ seyyasakaṁ ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.6
Pali: Āyasmā seyyasako hatthena upakkamitvā asuciṁ mocesi, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.7
Pali: Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.8
Pali: Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.9
Pali: Anuppannapaññatti tasmiṁ natthi. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.10
Pali: Sabbattha paññatti, padesapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.11
Pali: Sabbatthapaññatti.

Pali: Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.13

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.14
Pali: Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.15
Pali: Ekatopaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.16
Pali: Pañcannaṁ pātimokkhuddesānaṁ katthogadhaṁ kattha pariyāpannanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.17

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.18
Pali: Katamena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.19

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.21

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.23

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.28

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.36

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.38
Pali: Kā sampattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.39
Pali: Saṁvaro sampatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.40
Pali: Kā paṭipattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:27.41

pli-tv-pvr1.1:51.5

pli-tv-pvr1.1:51.7

pli-tv-pvr1.1:51.8

pli-tv-pvr1.1:60.0
Pali: 3. Aniyatakaṇḍa 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:60.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamo aniyato kattha paññatto? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:60.2
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbha? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:60.3
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusmiṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:60.4
Pali: Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññatti, sabbatthapaññatti padesapaññatti, sādhāraṇapaññatti asādhāraṇapaññatti, ekatopaññatti ubhatopaññatti, pañcannaṁ pātimokkhuddesānaṁ katthogadhaṁ kattha pariyāpannaṁ, katamena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchati, catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ katamā vipatti, sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katamo āpattikkhandho, channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti, catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ, sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammati, ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayo, kiṁ tattha pātimokkhaṁ, kiṁ tattha adhipātimokkhaṁ, kā vipatti, kā sampatti, kā paṭipatti, kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññatto, ke sikkhanti, ke sikkhitasikkhā, kattha ṭhitaṁ, ke dhārenti, kassa vacanaṁ kenābhatanti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena paṭhamo aniyato kattha paññattoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.2
Pali: Sāvatthiyaṁ paññatto. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.4
Pali: Āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.6
Pali: Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmena saddhiṁ eko ekāya raho paṭicchanne āsane alaṅkammaniye nisajjaṁ kappesi, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.7
Pali: Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.8
Pali: Ekā paññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.9
Pali: Anupaññatti anuppannapaññatti tasmiṁ natthi. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.10
Pali: Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.11
Pali: Sabbatthapaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.12
Pali: Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.13
Pali: Asādhāraṇapaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.14
Pali: Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.15
Pali: Ekatopaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.16
Pali: Pañcannaṁ pātimokkhuddesānaṁ katthogadhaṁ kattha pariyāpannanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.17
Pali: Nidānogadhaṁ nidānapariyāpannaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.18
Pali: Katamena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.19
Pali: Catutthena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.20
Pali: Catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ katamā vipattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.21
Pali: Siyā sīlavipatti siyā ācāravipatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.22
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.23
Pali: Siyā pārājikāpattikkhandho siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandho. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.24
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.25
Pali: Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti—

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.26
Pali: kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.27
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.28
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.29
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.30
Pali: Tīhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.31
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.32
Pali: Ko tattha vinayo, ko tattha abhivinayoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.33
Pali: Paññatti vinayo, vibhatti abhivinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.34
Pali: Kiṁ tattha pātimokkhaṁ, kiṁ tattha adhipātimokkhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.35
Pali: Paññatti pātimokkhaṁ, vibhatti adhipātimokkhaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.36
Pali: Kā vipattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.37
Pali: Asaṁvaro vipatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.38
Pali: Kā sampattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.39
Pali: Saṁvaro sampatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.40
Pali: Kā paṭipattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.41
Pali: Na evarūpaṁ karissāmīti yāvajīvaṁ āpāṇakoṭikaṁ samādāya sikkhati sikkhāpadesu. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.42
Pali: Kati atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññattoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.43
Pali: Dasa atthavase paṭicca bhagavatā paṭhamo aniyato paññatto—

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.44
Pali: saṅghasuṭṭhutāya, saṅghaphāsutāya, dummaṅkūnaṁ puggalānaṁ niggahāya, pesalānaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ phāsuvihārāya, diṭṭhadhammikānaṁ āsavānaṁ saṁvarāya, samparāyikānaṁ āsavānaṁ paṭighātāya, appasannānaṁ pasādāya, pasannānaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā, vinayānuggahāya. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.45
Pali: Ke sikkhantīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.46
Pali: Sekkhā ca puthujjanakalyāṇakā ca sikkhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.47
Pali: Ke sikkhitasikkhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.48
Pali: Arahanto sikkhitasikkhā. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.49
Pali: Kattha ṭhitanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.50
Pali: Sikkhākāmesu ṭhitaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.51
Pali: Ke dhārentīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.52
Pali: Yesaṁ vattati te dhārenti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.53
Pali: Kassa vacananti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.54
Pali: Bhagavato vacanaṁ arahato sammāsambuddhassa. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:61.55
Pali: Kenābhatanti?

pli-tv-pvr1.1:125.2
Pali: Sāvatthiyaṁ paññattaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:125.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:125.4
Pali: Āyasmantaṁ udāyiṁ ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:125.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.1:125.6
Pali: Āyasmā udāyī mātugāmassa dhammaṁ desesi, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ.

Pali: Ekā paññatti, dve anupaññattiyo.

Pali: 6. Pāṭidesanīyakaṇḍa 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:154.1
Pali: Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaṁ vā bhojanīyaṁ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjanto kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:154.2
Pali: Aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaṁ vā bhojanīyaṁ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjanto dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:154.3
Pali: “Bhuñjissāmī”ti paṭiggaṇhāti, āpatti dukkaṭassa; 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:154.4
Pali: ajjhohāre ajjhohāre āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa—

pli-tv-pvr1.2:154.5
Pali: aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaṁ vā bhojanīyaṁ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjanto imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:155.1
Pali: Bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjanto dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:155.2
Pali: “Bhuñjissāmī”ti paṭiggaṇhāti, āpatti dukkaṭassa; 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:155.3
Pali: ajjhohāre ajjhohāre āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa. 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:156.1
Pali: Sekkhasammatesu kulesu khādanīyaṁ vā bhojanīyaṁ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjanto dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.2:156.2

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena adinnaṁ ādiyanapaccayā pārājikaṁ kattha paññattanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.2
Pali: Rājagahe paññattaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.4
Pali: Dhaniyaṁ kumbhakāraputtaṁ ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.6
Pali: Dhaniyo kumbhakāraputto rañño dārūni adinnaṁ ādiyi, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.7
Pali: Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.8
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhāti—

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.9
Pali: siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.10
Pali: siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:6.11
Pali: siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti …pe…. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.1
Pali: Sañcicca manussaviggahaṁ jīvitā voropanapaccayā pārājikaṁ kattha paññattanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.2
Pali: Vesāliyaṁ paññattaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.4
Pali: Sambahule bhikkhū ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.6
Pali: Sambahulā bhikkhū aññamaññaṁ jīvitā voropesuṁ, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.7
Pali: Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:7.8

pli-tv-pvr1.9:8.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti?

pli-tv-pvr1.9:10.0
Pali: 2. Saṅghādisesakaṇḍādi 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:10.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena upakkamitvā asuciṁ mocanapaccayā saṅghādiseso kattha paññatto, kaṁ ārabbha, kismiṁ vatthusmiṁ …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:10.2
Pali: kenābhatanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.1
Pali: Yaṁ tena bhagavatā jānatā passatā arahatā sammāsambuddhena upakkamitvā asuciṁ mocanapaccayā saṅghādiseso kattha paññattoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.2
Pali: Sāvatthiyaṁ paññatto. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.3
Pali: Kaṁ ārabbhāti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.4
Pali: Āyasmantaṁ seyyasakaṁ ārabbha. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.5
Pali: Kismiṁ vatthusminti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.6
Pali: Āyasmā seyyasako upakkamitvā asuciṁ mocesi, tasmiṁ vatthusmiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.7
Pali: Atthi tattha paññatti, anupaññatti, anuppannapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.8
Pali: Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.9
Pali: Anuppannapaññatti tasmiṁ natthi. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.10
Pali: Sabbatthapaññatti, padesapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.11
Pali: Sabbatthapaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.12
Pali: Sādhāraṇapaññatti, asādhāraṇapaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.13
Pali: Asādhāraṇapaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.14
Pali: Ekatopaññatti, ubhatopaññattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.15
Pali: Ekatopaññatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.16
Pali: Pañcannaṁ pātimokkhuddesānaṁ katthogadhaṁ kattha pariyāpannanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.17
Pali: Nidānogadhaṁ nidānapariyāpannaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.18
Pali: Katamena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.19
Pali: Tatiyena uddesena uddesaṁ āgacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.20
Pali: Catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ katamā vipattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.21
Pali: Sīlavipatti. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.22
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katamo āpattikkhandhoti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.23
Pali: Saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho. 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.24
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhātīti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.25
Pali: Ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti—

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.26
Pali: kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.27
Pali: kenābhatanti? 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:11.28
Pali: Paramparābhataṁ—

Pali: Upāli dāsako ceva,

Pali: soṇako siggavo tathā;

Pali: Moggaliputtena pañcamā, 

pli-tv-pvr1.9:12.4
Pali: ete jambusirivhaye.

pli-tv-pvr1.9:26.7
Pali: Ekā paññatti.

pli-tv-pvr1.9:27.2
Pali: Sāvatthiyaṁ paññattaṁ.

Pali: Ekā paññatti, ekā anupaññatti.

pli-tv-pvr4:1.4

pli-tv-pvr4:2.1
Pali: Pañca āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.2
Pali: Pañca āpattikkhandhā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.3
Pali: Pañca vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.4
Pali: Satta āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.5
Pali: Satta āpattikkhandhā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.6
Pali: Satta vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.7
Pali: Cha agāravā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.8
Pali: Cha gāravā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.9
Pali: Cha vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.10
Pali: Catasso vipattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.11
Pali: Cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.12
Pali: Cha vivādamūlāni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.13
Pali: Cha anuvādamūlāni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.14
Pali: Cha sāraṇīyā dhammā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.15
Pali: Aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.16
Pali: Cattāri adhikaraṇāni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:2.17
Pali: Satta samathā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:3.1
Pali: Tattha katamā pañca āpattiyo? 

pli-tv-pvr4:3.2
Pali: Pārājikāpatti, saṅghādisesāpatti, pācittiyāpatti, pāṭidesanīyāpatti, dukkaṭāpatti—

pli-tv-pvr4:3.3
Pali: imā pañca āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:4.1
Pali: Tattha katame pañca āpattikkhandhā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:4.2
Pali: Pārājikāpattikkhandho, saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho, pācittiyāpattikkhandho, pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandho, dukkaṭāpattikkhandho—

pli-tv-pvr4:4.3
Pali: ime pañca āpattikkhandhā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:5.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni pañca vinītavatthūni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:5.2
Pali: Pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇī akiriyā akaraṇaṁ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto—

pli-tv-pvr4:5.3
Pali: imāni pañca vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:6.1
Pali: Tattha katamā satta āpattiyo? 

pli-tv-pvr4:6.2
Pali: Pārājikāpatti, saṅghādisesāpatti, thullaccayāpatti, pācittiyāpatti, pāṭidesanīyāpatti, dukkaṭāpatti, dubbhāsitāpatti—

pli-tv-pvr4:6.3
Pali: imā satta āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:7.1
Pali: Tattha katame satta āpattikkhandhā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:7.2
Pali: Pārājikāpattikkhandho, saṅghādisesāpattikkhandho, thullaccayāpattikkhandho, pācittiyāpattikkhandho, pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandho, dukkaṭāpattikkhandho, dubbhāsitāpattikkhandho—

pli-tv-pvr4:7.3
Pali: ime satta āpattikkhandhā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:8.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni satta vinītavatthūni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:8.2
Pali: Sattahi āpattikkhandhehi ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇī akiriyā akaraṇaṁ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto—

pli-tv-pvr4:8.3
Pali: imāni satta vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:9.1
Pali: Tattha katame cha agāravā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:9.2
Pali: Buddhe agāravo, dhamme agāravo, saṅghe agāravo, sikkhāya agāravo, appamāde agāravo, paṭisandhāre agāravo—

pli-tv-pvr4:9.3
Pali: ime cha agāravā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:10.1
Pali: Tattha katame cha gāravā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:10.2
Pali: Buddhe gāravo, dhamme gāravo, saṅghe gāravo, sikkhāya gāravo, appamāde gāravo, paṭisandhāre gāravo—

pli-tv-pvr4:10.3
Pali: ime cha gāravā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:11.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni cha vinītavatthūni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:11.2
Pali: Chahi agāravehi ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇī akiriyā akaraṇaṁ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto—

pli-tv-pvr4:11.3
Pali: imāni cha vinītavatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:12.1
Pali: Tattha katamā catasso vipattiyo? 

pli-tv-pvr4:12.2
Pali: Sīlavipatti, ācāravipatti, diṭṭhivipatti, ājīvavipatti—

pli-tv-pvr4:12.3
Pali: imā catasso vipattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.1
Pali: Tattha katame cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.2
Pali: Atthāpatti kāyato samuṭṭhāti, na vācato na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.3
Pali: atthāpatti vācato samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.4
Pali: atthāpatti kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhāti, na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.5
Pali: atthāpatti kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na vācato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.6
Pali: atthāpatti vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti, na kāyato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:13.7
Pali: atthāpatti kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti—

pli-tv-pvr4:13.8
Pali: ime cha āpattisamuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni cha vivādamūlāni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu kodhano hoti upanāhī. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.3
Pali: Yo so bhikkhu kodhano hoti upanāhī so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatisso, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatisso, saṅghepi agāravo viharati appatisso, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakārī hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.4
Pali: Yo so bhikkhu satthari agāravo viharati appatisso, dhamme …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.5
Pali: saṅghe …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.6
Pali: sikkhāya na paripūrakārī, so saṅghe vivādaṁ janeti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.7
Pali: Yo hoti vivādo bahujanāhitāya bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.8
Pali: Evarūpañce tumhe vivādamūlaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.9
Pali: Evarūpañce tumhe vivādamūlaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā na samanupasseyyātha tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiṁ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.10
Pali: Evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaṁ hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:14.11
Pali: Evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiṁ anavassavo hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhu makkhī hoti paḷāsī …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.2
Pali: issukī hoti maccharī, saṭho hoti māyāvī, pāpiccho hoti micchādiṭṭhi, sandiṭṭhiparāmāsī hoti ādhānaggāhī duppaṭinissaggī. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.3
Pali: Yo so bhikkhu sandiṭṭhiparāmāsī hoti ādhānaggāhī duppaṭinissaggī so sattharipi agāravo viharati appatisso, dhammepi agāravo viharati appatisso, saṅghepi agāravo viharati appatisso, sikkhāyapi na paripūrakārī hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.4
Pali: Yo so bhikkhu satthari agāravo viharati appatisso dhamme …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.5
Pali: saṅghe …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.6
Pali: sikkhāya na paripūrakārī, so saṅghe vivādaṁ janeti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.7
Pali: Yo so hoti vivādo bahujanāhitāya bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.8
Pali: Evarūpañce tumhe vivādamūlaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā samanupasseyyātha tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānāya vāyameyyātha. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.9
Pali: Evarūpañce tumhe vivādamūlaṁ ajjhattaṁ vā bahiddhā vā na samanupasseyyātha tatra tumhe tasseva pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiṁ anavassavāya paṭipajjeyyātha. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.10
Pali: Evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa pahānaṁ hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.11
Pali: Evametassa pāpakassa vivādamūlassa āyatiṁ anavassavo hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:15.12
Pali: Imāni cha vivādamūlāni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:16.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni cha anuvādamūlāni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:16.2

Pali: Evametassa pāpakassa anuvādamūlassa āyatiṁ anavassavo hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:17.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhu makkhī hoti palāsī …pe…

Pali: issukī hoti maccharī, saṭho hoti māyāvī, pāpiccho hoti micchādiṭṭhi, sandiṭṭhiparāmāsī hoti ādhānaggāhī duppaṭinissaggī.

pli-tv-pvr4:18.1
Pali: Tattha katame cha sāraṇīyā dhammā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:18.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhuno mettaṁ kāyakammaṁ paccupaṭṭhitaṁ hoti sabrahmacārīsu āvi ceva raho ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:18.3
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:19.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhuno mettaṁ vacīkammaṁ paccupaṭṭhitaṁ hoti sabrahmacārīsu āvi ceva raho ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:19.2
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:20.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhuno mettaṁ manokammaṁ paccupaṭṭhitaṁ hoti sabrahmacārīsu āvi ceva raho ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:20.2
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:21.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhu ye te lābhā dhammikā dhammaladdhā antamaso pattapariyāpannamattampi tathārūpehi lābhehi appaṭivibhattabhogī hoti sīlavantehi sabrahmacārīhi sādhāraṇabhogī. 

pli-tv-pvr4:21.2
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:22.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhu yāni tāni sīlāni akhaṇḍāni acchiddāni asabalāni akammāsāni bhujissāni viññupasatthāni aparāmaṭṭhāni samādhisaṁvattanikāni, tathārūpesu sīlesu sīlasāmaññagato viharati sabrahmacārīhi āvi ceva raho ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:22.2
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:23.1
Pali: Puna caparaṁ bhikkhu yāyaṁ diṭṭhi ariyā niyyānikā niyyāti takkarassa sammā dukkhakkhayāya tathārūpāya diṭṭhiyā diṭṭhisāmaññagato viharati sabrahmacārīhi āvi ceva raho ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:23.2
Pali: Ayampi dhammo sāraṇīyo piyakaraṇo garukaraṇo saṅgahāya avivādāya sāmaggiyā ekībhāvāya saṁvattati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:23.3
Pali: Ime cha sāraṇīyā dhammā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:24.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:24.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu adhammaṁ “dhammo”ti dīpeti, dhammaṁ “adhammo”ti dīpeti, avinayaṁ “vinayo”ti dīpeti, vinayaṁ “avinayo”ti dīpeti, abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatena “bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatena “abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena “āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena “anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, apaññattaṁ tathāgatena “paññattaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, paññattaṁ tathāgatena “apaññattaṁ tathāgatenā”ti dīpeti, āpattiṁ “anāpattī”ti dīpeti, anāpattiṁ “āpattī”ti dīpeti, lahukaṁ āpattiṁ “garukā āpattī”ti dīpeti, garukaṁ āpattiṁ “lahukā āpattī”ti dīpeti, sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ “anavasesā āpattī”ti dīpeti, anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ “sāvasesā āpattī”ti dīpeti, duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ “aduṭṭhullā āpattī”ti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ “duṭṭhullā āpattī”ti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:24.3
Pali: Imāni aṭṭhārasa bhedakaravatthūni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:25.1
Pali: Tattha katamāni cattāri adhikaraṇāni? 

pli-tv-pvr4:25.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, kiccādhikaraṇaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr4:25.3
Pali: imāni cattāri adhikaraṇāni. 

pli-tv-pvr4:26.1
Pali: Tattha katame satta samathā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:26.2
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, yebhuyyasikā, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako—

pli-tv-pvr4:26.3
Pali: ime satta samathā. 

pli-tv-pvr4:27.1
Pali: Katipucchāvāro niṭṭhito. 

pli-tv-pvr4:28.1
Pali: Tassuddānaṁ 

pli-tv-pvr4:29.1
Pali: Āpatti āpattikkhandhā, 

pli-tv-pvr4:29.2
Pali: vinītā sattadhā puna; 

pli-tv-pvr4:29.3
Pali: Vinītāgāravā ceva, 

pli-tv-pvr4:29.4
Pali: gāravā mūlameva ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.1
Pali: Puna vinītā vipatti, 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.2
Pali: samuṭṭhānā vivādanā; 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.3
Pali: Anuvādā sāraṇīyaṁ, 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.4
Pali: bhedādhikaraṇena ca; 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.5
Pali: Satteva samathā vuttā, 

pli-tv-pvr4:30.6
Pali: padā sattarasā imeti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.0
Pali: 4.1. Chaāpattisamuṭṭhānavāra 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.1
Pali: Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pārājikaṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.2
Pali: Na hīti vattabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.3
Pali: Saṅghādisesaṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.4
Pali: Siyāti vattabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.5
Pali: Thullaccayaṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.6
Pali: Siyāti vattabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.7
Pali: Pācittiyaṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.8
Pali: Siyāti vattabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.9
Pali: Pāṭidesanīyaṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.10
Pali: Siyāti vattabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:31.11
Pali: Dukkaṭaṁ āpajjeyyāti?

pli-tv-pvr4:37.1
Pali: Chaāpattisamuṭṭhānavāro niṭṭhito paṭhamo. 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.0
Pali: 4.2. Katāpattivāra 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.1
Pali: Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.2
Pali: Paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pañca āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.3
Pali: Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī saññācikāya kuṭiṁ karoti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ, payoge dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.4
Pali: ekaṁ piṇḍaṁ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.5
Pali: tasmiṁ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saṅghādisesassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.6
Pali: bhikkhu kappiyasaññī vikāle bhojanaṁ bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:38.7
Pali: bhikkhu kappiyasaññī aññātikāya bhikkhuniyā antaragharaṁ paviṭṭhāya hatthato khādanīyaṁ vā bhojanīyaṁ vā sahatthā paṭiggahetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:38.8
Pali: paṭhamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.2
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.3
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.4
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.6
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:39.7
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.8
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:39.9
Pali: siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.10
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:39.11
Pali: kāyato samuṭṭhanti, na vācato na cittato. 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.12
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:39.13
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:39.14
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:40.1
Pali: Dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:40.2
Pali: Dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena catasso āpattiyo āpajjati—

pli-tv-pvr4:40.3
Pali: bhikkhu kappiyasaññī samādisati—“kuṭiṁ me karothā”ti. Tassa kuṭiṁ karonti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ. Payoge dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr4:40.4
Pali: ekaṁ piṇḍaṁ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:40.5
Pali: tasmiṁ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saṅghādisesassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:40.6
Pali: Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī anupasampannaṁ padaso dhammaṁ vāceti, āpatti pācittiyassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:40.7
Pali: dutiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.2
Pali: sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.3
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:41.4
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:41.6
Pali: siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.7

pli-tv-pvr4:41.8
Pali: vācato samuṭṭhanti, na kāyato na cittato.

Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:41.10
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:41.11
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.1
Pali: Tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.2
Pali: Tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena pañca āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.3
Pali: Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī saṁvidahitvā kuṭiṁ karoti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ. Payoge dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.4
Pali: ekaṁ piṇḍaṁ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.5
Pali: tasmiṁ piṇḍe āgate āpatti saṅghādisesassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.6
Pali: Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:42.7
Pali: Bhikkhu kappiyasaññī bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:42.8
Pali: tatiyena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati.

pli-tv-pvr4:44.1

pli-tv-pvr4:44.3
Pali: bhikkhu methunaṁ dhammaṁ paṭisevati, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:44.4
Pali: bhikkhu akappiyasaññī saññācikāya kuṭiṁ karoti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ, payoge dukkaṭaṁ;

pli-tv-pvr4:46.1

pli-tv-pvr4:46.2
Pali: Pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena cha āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:46.3
Pali: Bhikkhu pāpiccho icchāpakato asantaṁ abhūtaṁ uttarimanussadhammaṁ ullapati, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:46.4
Pali: bhikkhu akappiyasaññī samādisati—“kuṭiṁ me karothā”ti. Tassa kuṭiṁ karonti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ. Payoge dukkaṭaṁ;

pli-tv-pvr4:46.7
Pali: Bhikkhu akappiyasaññī anupasampannaṁ padaso dhammaṁ vāceti, āpatti pācittiyassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:46.8
Pali: Na khuṁsetukāmo na vambhetukāmo na maṅkukattukāmo davakamyatā hīnena hīnaṁ vadeti, āpatti dubbhāsitassa—

Pali: pañcamena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati.

Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ.

Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:47.11
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.1
Pali: Chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.2
Pali: Chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena cha āpattiyo āpajjati—

pli-tv-pvr4:48.3
Pali: bhikkhu saṁvidahitvā bhaṇḍaṁ avaharati, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.4
Pali: bhikkhu akappiyasaññī saṁvidahitvā kuṭiṁ karoti adesitavatthukaṁ pamāṇātikkantaṁ sārambhaṁ aparikkamanaṁ, payoge dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.5
Pali: ekaṁ piṇḍaṁ anāgate āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.6
Pali: tasmiṁ piṇḍe āgate, āpatti saṅghādisesassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.7
Pali: Bhikkhu akappiyasaññī paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa. 

pli-tv-pvr4:48.8
Pali: Bhikkhu akappiyasaññī bhikkhuniyā vosāsantiyā na nivāretvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:48.9
Pali: chaṭṭhena āpattisamuṭṭhānena imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.2
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.3
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi āpattisamuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.4
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.6
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:49.7
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.8
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:49.9
Pali: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena, siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.10
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:49.11
Pali: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.12
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:49.13
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:49.14
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena cāti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:50.1
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katāpattivāro niṭṭhito dutiyo.

pli-tv-pvr4:64.0
Pali: 4.4. Vipattipaccayavāra 

pli-tv-pvr4:64.1
Pali: Sīlavipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:64.2
Pali: Sīlavipattipaccayā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati—

pli-tv-pvr4:64.3
Pali: bhikkhunī jānaṁ pārājikaṁ dhammaṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:64.4
Pali: vematikā paṭicchādeti, āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:64.5
Pali: bhikkhu saṅghādisesaṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:64.6
Pali: attano duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:64.7
Pali: sīlavipattipaccayā imā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.2
Pali: sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.3
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:65.4
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:65.6
Pali: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.7
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:65.8
Pali: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.9
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:65.10
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:65.11
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:66.1
Pali: Ācāravipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:66.2
Pali: Ācāravipattipaccayā ekaṁ āpattiṁ āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:66.3
Pali: Ācāravipattiṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:66.4
Pali: ācāravipattipaccayā imaṁ ekaṁ āpattiṁ āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.1
Pali: Sā āpatti catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajati …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.2
Pali: sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.3
Pali: Sā āpatti catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ ekaṁ vipattiṁ bhajati—

pli-tv-pvr4:67.4
Pali: ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ ekena āpattikkhandhena saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:67.6
Pali: dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.7
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhāti—

pli-tv-pvr4:67.8
Pali: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhāti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.9
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:67.10
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr4:67.11
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:68.1
Pali: Diṭṭhivipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:68.2
Pali: Diṭṭhivipattipaccayā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:68.3
Pali: Pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāvatatiyaṁ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjati, ñattiyā dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr4:68.4
Pali: kammavācāpariyosāne āpatti pācittiyassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:68.5
Pali: diṭṭhivipattipaccayā imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.2
Pali: sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.3
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ ekaṁ vipattiṁ bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:69.4
Pali: ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ dvīhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:69.6
Pali: siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.7
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:69.8

pli-tv-pvr4:69.9
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:69.10
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:69.11
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.1
Pali: Ājīvavipattipaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.2
Pali: Ājīvavipattipaccayā cha āpattiyo āpajjati—

pli-tv-pvr4:70.3
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā pāpiccho icchāpakato asantaṁ abhūtaṁ uttarimanussadhammaṁ ullapati, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.4
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā sañcarittaṁ samāpajjati, āpatti saṅghādisesassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.5
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā “yo te vihāre vasati, so bhikkhu arahā”ti bhaṇati, paṭivijānantassa āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.6
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā bhikkhu paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.7
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā bhikkhunī paṇītabhojanāni attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti pāṭidesanīyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:70.8
Pali: ājīvahetu ājīvakāraṇā sūpaṁ vā odanaṁ vā agilāno attano atthāya viññāpetvā bhuñjati, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:70.9
Pali: ājīvavipattipaccayā imā cha āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.2
Pali: sattannaṁ samathānaṁ katihi samathehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.3
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:71.4
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ chahi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:71.6
Pali: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena, siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā pāṭidesanīyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.7
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ chahi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:71.8
Pali: siyā kāyato samuṭṭhanti, na vācato na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.9
Pali: siyā vācato samuṭṭhanti, na kāyato na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.10
Pali: siyā kāyato ca vācato ca samuṭṭhanti, na cittato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.11
Pali: siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti, na vācato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.12
Pali: siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti, na kāyato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.13
Pali: siyā kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.14
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:71.15
Pali: Sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:71.16
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr4:72.1
Pali: Vipattipaccayavāro niṭṭhito catuttho. 

pli-tv-pvr4:73.0
Pali: 4.5. Adhikaraṇapaccayavāra 

pli-tv-pvr4:73.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr4:73.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā dve āpattiyo āpajjati—

pli-tv-pvr4:73.3
Pali: upasampannaṁ omasati, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr4:73.4
Pali: anupasampannaṁ omasati, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr4:73.5
Pali: vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr4:74.1

pli-tv-pvr4:74.4
Pali: ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr4:74.5
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ dvīhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr4:74.6
Pali: siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr4:74.7
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr4:74.8
Pali: siyā kāyato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti, na vācato; 

pli-tv-pvr4:74.9
Pali: siyā vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti, na kāyato;

Pali: Sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, yebhuyyasikā, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako—

pli-tv-pvr5:9.4
Pali: ime satta samathā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:10.1
Pali: Siyā ime satta samathā dasa samathā honti, dasa samathā satta samathā honti vatthuvasena pariyāyena? 

pli-tv-pvr5:10.2
Pali: Siyāti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:11.1
Pali: Kathañca siyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:11.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇassa dve samathā, anuvādādhikaraṇassa cattāro samathā, āpattādhikaraṇassa tayo samathā, kiccādhikaraṇassa eko samatho. 

pli-tv-pvr5:11.3
Pali: Evaṁ ime satta samathā dasa samathā honti, dasa samathā satta samathā honti vatthuvasena pariyāyena. 

pli-tv-pvr5:12.1
Pali: Pariyāyavāro niṭṭhito chaṭṭho. 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.0
Pali: 2. Sādhāraṇavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.1
Pali: Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.2
Pali: Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.3
Pali: Kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.4
Pali: Kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.5
Pali: Kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.6
Pali: Kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.7
Pali: Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:13.8
Pali: Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:14.1
Pali: Dve samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:14.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, yebhuyyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:14.3
Pali: Pañca samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:14.4
Pali: sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:15.1
Pali: Cattāro samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:15.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:15.3
Pali: Tayo samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:15.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:16.1
Pali: Tayo samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:16.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:16.3
Pali: Cattāro samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:16.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:17.1
Pali: Eko samatho kiccādhikaraṇassa sādhāraṇo—

pli-tv-pvr5:17.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:17.3
Pali: Cha samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa asādhāraṇā—

pli-tv-pvr5:17.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:18.1
Pali: Sādhāraṇavāro niṭṭhito sattamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.0
Pali: 3. Tabbhāgiyavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.1
Pali: Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.2
Pali: Kati samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.3
Pali: Kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.4
Pali: Kati samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.5
Pali: Kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.6
Pali: Kati samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.7
Pali: Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:19.8
Pali: Kati samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:20.1
Pali: Dve samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:20.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, yebhuyyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:20.3
Pali: Pañca samathā vivādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:20.4
Pali: sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:21.1
Pali: Cattāro samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:21.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:21.3
Pali: Tayo samathā anuvādādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:21.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:22.1
Pali: Tayo samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:22.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:22.3
Pali: Cattāro samathā āpattādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:22.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:23.1
Pali: Eko samatho kiccādhikaraṇassa tabbhāgiyo—

pli-tv-pvr5:23.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:23.3
Pali: Cha samathā kiccādhikaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā—

pli-tv-pvr5:23.4
Pali: yebhuyyasikā, sativinayo, amūḷhavinayo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, tassapāpiyasikā, tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:24.1
Pali: Tabbhāgiyavāro niṭṭhito aṭṭhamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:25.0
Pali: 4. Samathāsamathassasādhāraṇavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:25.1
Pali: Samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā, samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:25.2
Pali: Siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā, siyā samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:26.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:26.2
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:26.3
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇā, sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa asādhāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:27.1
Pali: Sativinayo sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya asādhāraṇo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:28.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa asādhāraṇo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:29.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇaṁ, tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa asādhāraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:30.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇā, tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa asādhāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:31.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayassa sādhāraṇo, yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya asādhāraṇo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:32.1
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā samathassa sādhāraṇā; 

pli-tv-pvr5:32.2
Pali: evaṁ siyā samathā samathassa asādhāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:33.1
Pali: Samathā samathassa sādhāraṇavāro niṭṭhito navamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:34.0
Pali: 5. Samathāsamathassatabbhāgiyavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:34.1
Pali: Samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:34.2
Pali: Siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:35.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:35.2
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:35.3
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyā, sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa aññabhāgiyā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:36.1
Pali: Sativinayo sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyo, amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya aññabhāgiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:37.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyo, paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa aññabhāgiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:38.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyaṁ, tassapāpiyasikāya tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa aññabhāgiyaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:39.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyā, tiṇavatthārakassa yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa aññabhāgiyā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:40.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayassa tabbhāgiyo, yebhuyyasikāya sativinayassa amūḷhavinayassa paṭiññātakaraṇassa tassapāpiyasikāya aññabhāgiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:41.1
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyā, evaṁ siyā samathā samathassa aññabhāgiyā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:42.1
Pali: Samathā samathassa tabbhāgiyavāro niṭṭhito dasamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.0
Pali: 6. Samathasammukhāvinayavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.1
Pali: Samatho sammukhāvinayo, sammukhāvinayo samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.2
Pali: Samatho yebhuyyasikā, yebhuyyasikā samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.3
Pali: Samatho sativinayo, sativinayo samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.4
Pali: Samatho amūḷhavinayo, amūḷhavinayo samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.5
Pali: Samatho paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.6
Pali: Samatho tassapāpiyasikā, tassapāpiyasikā samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:43.7
Pali: Samatho tiṇavatthārako, tiṇavatthārako samatho? 

pli-tv-pvr5:44.1
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tassapāpiyasikā tiṇavatthārako—

pli-tv-pvr5:44.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no sammukhāvinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:44.3
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo samatho ceva sammukhāvinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:45.1
Pali: Sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tassapāpiyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo—

pli-tv-pvr5:45.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no yebhuyyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:45.3
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā samatho ceva yebhuyyasikā ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:46.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tassapāpiyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā—

pli-tv-pvr5:46.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no sativinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:46.3
Pali: Sativinayo samatho ceva sativinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:47.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tassapāpiyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo—

pli-tv-pvr5:47.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no amūḷhavinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:47.3
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo samatho ceva amūḷhavinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:48.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo—

pli-tv-pvr5:48.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:48.3
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ samatho ceva paṭiññātakaraṇañca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:49.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr5:49.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:49.3
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā samatho ceva tassapāpiyasikā ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:50.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo yebhuyyasikā sativinayo amūḷhavinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tassapāpiyasikā—

pli-tv-pvr5:50.2
Pali: ime samathā samathā, no tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:50.3
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako samatho ceva tiṇavatthārako ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:51.1
Pali: Samathasammukhāvinayavāro niṭṭhito ekādasamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.0
Pali: 7. Vinayavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.1
Pali: Vinayo sammukhāvinayo, sammukhāvinayo vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.2
Pali: Vinayo yebhuyyasikā, yebhuyyasikā vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.3
Pali: Vinayo sativinayo, sativinayo vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.4
Pali: Vinayo amūḷhavinayo, amūḷhavinayo vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.5
Pali: Vinayo paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.6
Pali: Vinayo tassapāpiyasikā, tassapāpiyasikā vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:52.7
Pali: Vinayo tiṇavatthārako, tiṇavatthārako vinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr5:53.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā sammukhāvinayo siyā na sammukhāvinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:53.2
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo vinayo ceva sammukhāvinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:54.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā yebhuyyasikā, siyā na yebhuyyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:54.2
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā vinayo ceva yebhuyyasikā ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:55.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā sativinayo, siyā na sativinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:55.2
Pali: Sativinayo vinayo ceva sativinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:56.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā amūḷhavinayo, siyā na amūḷhavinayo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:56.2
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo vinayo ceva amūḷhavinayo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:57.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, siyā na paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:57.2
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ vinayo ceva paṭiññātakaraṇañca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:58.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā tassapāpiyasikā, siyā na tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:58.2
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā vinayo ceva tassapāpiyasikā ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:59.1
Pali: Vinayo siyā tiṇavatthārako, siyā na tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr5:59.2
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako vinayo ceva tiṇavatthārako ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:60.1
Pali: Vinayavāro niṭṭhito dvādasamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.0
Pali: 8. Kusalavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.2
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā kusalā akusalā abyākatā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.3
Pali: Sativinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.4
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo kusalo akusalo abyākato? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.5
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ kusalaṁ akusalaṁ abyākataṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.6
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā kusalā akusalā abyākatā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:61.7
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako kusalo akusalo abyākato? 

pli-tv-pvr5:62.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo siyā kusalo, siyā abyākato. 

pli-tv-pvr5:62.2
Pali: Natthi sammukhāvinayo akusalo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:63.1
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā siyā kusalā, siyā akusalā, siyā abyākatā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:64.1
Pali: Sativinayo siyā kusalo, siyā akusalo, siyā abyākato. 

pli-tv-pvr5:65.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo siyā kusalo, siyā akusalo, siyā abyākato. 

pli-tv-pvr5:66.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ siyā kusalaṁ, siyā akusalaṁ, siyā abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:67.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā siyā kusalā, siyā akusalā siyā abyākatā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:68.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako siyā kusalo, siyā akusalo, siyā abyākato. 

pli-tv-pvr5:69.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ kusalaṁ akusalaṁ abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:69.2
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ kusalaṁ akusalaṁ abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:69.3
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ kusalaṁ akusalaṁ abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:69.4
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ kusalaṁ akusalaṁ abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:70.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ siyā kusalaṁ, siyā akusalaṁ, siyā abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:71.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ siyā kusalaṁ, siyā akusalaṁ, siyā abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:72.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ siyā akusalaṁ, siyā abyākataṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:72.2

pli-tv-pvr5:73.1

pli-tv-pvr5:74.1

pli-tv-pvr5:92.0
Pali: 11. Saṁsaṭṭhavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:92.1
Pali: Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā udāhu visaṁsaṭṭhā? 

pli-tv-pvr5:92.2
Pali: Labbhā ca panimesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetunti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.1
Pali: Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā visaṁsaṭṭhā, no saṁsaṭṭhā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.2
Pali: Labbhā ca panimesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetunti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.3
Pali: So—“mā hevan”tissa vacanīyo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.4
Pali: Adhikaraṇanti vā samathāti vā ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā, no visaṁsaṭṭhā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.5
Pali: No ca labbhā imesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetuṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.6
Pali: Taṁ kissa hetu? 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.7
Pali: Nanu vuttaṁ bhagavatā—

pli-tv-pvr5:93.8
Pali: “cattārimāni, bhikkhave, adhikaraṇāni, satta samathā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.9
Pali: Adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti, samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.10
Pali: Evaṁ, ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā no visaṁsaṭṭhā; 

pli-tv-pvr5:93.11
Pali: no ca labbhā imesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetun”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:94.1
Pali: Saṁsaṭṭhavāro niṭṭhito soḷasamo.

pli-tv-pvr5:113.4

Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:118.3
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca dvīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:118.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:118.5
Pali: Pañcahi samathehi na sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:118.6
Pali: sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:119.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:119.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:119.3
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca chahi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:119.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:119.5
Pali: Ekena samathena na sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:119.6
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya. 

pli-tv-pvr5:120.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:120.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:120.3
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca catūhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:120.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:120.5
Pali: Tīhi samathehi na sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:120.6
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:121.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:121.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:121.3
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:121.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:121.5
Pali: Catūhi samathehi na sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:121.6
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:122.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:122.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:122.3
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca sattahi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:122.4
Pali: ammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:123.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:123.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:123.3
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇañca anuvādādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca pañcahi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:123.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:123.5
Pali: Dvīhi samathehi na sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:123.6
Pali: paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca.

Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇañca āpattādhikaraṇañca kiccādhikaraṇañca katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:124.2
Pali: Katihi samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:124.3

pli-tv-pvr5:124.4

pli-tv-pvr5:124.6

pli-tv-pvr5:126.1
Pali: Sammanti na sammantivāro niṭṭhito aṭṭhārasamo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:127.0
Pali: 14. Samathādhikaraṇavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:127.1
Pali: Samathā samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:127.2
Pali: Samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:127.3
Pali: Adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:127.4
Pali: Adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:128.1
Pali: Siyā samathā samathehi sammanti, siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:128.2
Pali: Siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti, siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:128.3
Pali: Siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti, siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:128.4
Pali: Siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti, siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:129.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā samathehi sammanti, kathaṁ siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:129.2
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:129.3
Pali: sativinayena na sammati, amūḷhavinayena na sammati, paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati, tassapāpiyasikāya na sammati, tiṇavatthārakena na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:130.1
Pali: Sativinayo sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:130.2
Pali: amūḷhavinayena na sammati, paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammāti, tassapāpiyasikāya na sammati, tiṇavatthārakena na sammati, yebhuyyasikāya na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:131.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:131.2
Pali: paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati, tassapāpiyasikāya na sammati, tiṇavatthārakena na sammati, yebhuyyasikāya na sammati, sativinayena na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:132.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:132.2
Pali: tassapāpiyasikāya na sammati, tiṇavatthārakena na sammati, yebhuyyasikāya na sammati, sativinayena na sammati, amūḷhavinayena na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:133.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:133.2
Pali: tiṇavatthārakena na sammati, yebhuyyasikāya na sammati, sativinayena na sammati, amūḷhavinayena na sammati, paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:134.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:134.2
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya na sammati, sativinayena na sammati, amūḷhavinayena na sammati, paṭiññātakaraṇena na sammati, tassapāpiyasikāya na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:134.3
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā samathehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:134.4
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā samathehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:135.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti, kathaṁ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:135.2
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:135.3
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:136.1
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:136.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:137.1
Pali: Sativinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:137.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:138.1
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:138.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:139.1
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:139.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:140.1
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:140.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:141.1
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:141.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:141.3
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:141.4
Pali: Evaṁ siyā samathā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:142.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti, kathaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:142.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:142.3
Pali: sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:143.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:143.2
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:144.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:144.2
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:145.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ sammukhāvinayena sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:145.2
Pali: yebhuyyasikāya ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca tiṇavatthārakena ca na sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:145.3
Pali: Evaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:145.4
Pali: Evaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā samathehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:146.1
Pali: Kathaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti? Kathaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:146.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:146.3
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:147.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:147.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:148.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:148.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:149.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ vivādādhikaraṇena na sammati, anuvādādhikaraṇena na sammati, āpattādhikaraṇena na sammati; 

pli-tv-pvr5:149.2
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:149.3
Pali: Evaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:149.4
Pali: Evaṁ siyā adhikaraṇā adhikaraṇehi na sammanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:150.1
Pali: Chāpi samathā cattāropi adhikaraṇā sammukhāvinayena sammanti; 

pli-tv-pvr5:150.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayo na kenaci sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:151.1
Pali: Samathādhikaraṇavāro niṭṭhito ekūnavīsatimo. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.0
Pali: 15. Samuṭṭhāpanavāra 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ na katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti; 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.3
Pali: api ca vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.5
Pali: Idha bhikkhū vivadanti—

pli-tv-pvr5:152.6
Pali: “dhammo”ti vā, “adhammo”ti vā, “vinayo”ti vā, “avinayo”ti vā, “abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “apaññattaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “paññattaṁ tathāgatenā”ti vā, “āpattī”ti vā, “anāpattī”ti vā, “lahukā āpattī”ti vā, “garukā āpattī”ti vā, “sāvasesā āpattī”ti vā, “anavasesā āpattī”ti vā, “duṭṭhullā āpattī”ti vā “aduṭṭhullā āpattī”ti vā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.7
Pali: Yaṁ tattha bhaṇḍanaṁ kalaho viggaho vivādo nānāvādo aññathāvādo vipaccatāya vohāro medhakaṁ, idaṁ vuccati vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.8
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.9
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ vivadamāno anuvadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.10
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.11
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:152.12
Pali: Evaṁ vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.2
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ na katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti; 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.3
Pali: api ca anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.5
Pali: Idha bhikkhū bhikkhuṁ anuvadanti sīlavipattiyā vā ācāravipattiyā vā diṭṭhivipattiyā vā ājīvavipattiyā vā. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.6
Pali: Yo tattha anuvādo anuvadanā anullapanā anubhaṇanā anusampavaṅkatā abbhussahanatā anubalappadānaṁ, idaṁ vuccati anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.7
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.8
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ vivadamāno anuvadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.9
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.10
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:153.11
Pali: Evaṁ anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.2
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ na katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti; 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.3
Pali: api ca āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.5
Pali: Pañcapi āpattikkhandhā āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, sattapi āpattikkhandhā āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, idaṁ vuccati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.6
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.7
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ vivadamāno anuvadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.8
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.9
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:154.10
Pali: Evaṁ āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti? 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.2
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ na katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ samuṭṭhāpeti, 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.3
Pali: api ca kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.5
Pali: Yā saṅghassa kiccayatā karaṇīyatā apalokanakammaṁ ñattikammaṁ ñattidutiyakammaṁ ñatticatutthakammaṁ, idaṁ vuccati kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.6
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.7
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ vivadamāno anuvadati. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.8
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.9
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr5:155.10
Pali: Evaṁ kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā cattāro adhikaraṇā jāyanti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:156.1
Pali: Samuṭṭhāpanavāro niṭṭhito vīsatimo.

pli-tv-pvr5:161.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ vivādādhikaraṇaṁ bhajati, vivādādhikaraṇaṁ upanissitaṁ, vivādādhikaraṇaṁ pariyāpannaṁ, vivādādhikaraṇena saṅgahitaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr5:165.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaṁ, kati samathe pariyāpannaṁ, katihi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ, katihi samathehi sammati?

Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaṁ, kati samathe pariyāpannaṁ, katihi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ, katihi samathehi sammati?

Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ kati samathe bhajati, kati samathe upanissitaṁ, kati samathe pariyāpannaṁ, katihi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ, katihi samathehi sammati? 

pli-tv-pvr5:169.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ dve samathe bhajati, dve samathe upanissitaṁ, dve samathe pariyāpannaṁ, dvīhi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ, dvīhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr5:169.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:170.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ cattāro samathe bhajati, cattāro samathe upanissitaṁ, cattāro samathe pariyāpannaṁ, catūhi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ, catūhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr5:170.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:171.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ tayo samathe bhajati, tayo samathe upanissitaṁ, tayo samathe pariyāpannaṁ, tīhi samathehi saṅgahitaṁ tīhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr5:171.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr5:172.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ sattannaṁ samathānaṁ ekaṁ samathaṁ bhajati, ekaṁ samathaṁ upanissitaṁ, ekaṁ samathaṁ pariyāpannaṁ, ekena samathena saṅgahitaṁ, ekena samathena sammati—

pli-tv-pvr5:172.2
Pali: sammukhāvinayenāti. 

pli-tv-pvr5:173.1
Pali: Bhajativāro niṭṭhito ekavīsatimo.

pli-tv-pvr7:7.0
Pali: 2. Dukavāra 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.1
Pali: Atthāpatti saññā vimokkhā, atthāpatti no saññāvimokkhā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.2
Pali: Atthāpatti laddhasamāpattikassa, atthāpatti na laddhasamāpattikassa. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.3
Pali: Atthāpatti saddhammapaṭisaññuttā, atthāpatti asaddhammapaṭisaññuttā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.4
Pali: Atthāpatti saparikkhārapaṭisaññuttā, atthāpatti paraparikkhārapaṭisaññuttā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.5
Pali: Atthāpatti sapuggalapaṭisaññuttā, atthāpatti parapuggalapaṭisaññuttā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.6

pli-tv-pvr7:7.7
Pali: Atthi musā bhaṇanto garukaṁ āpattiṁ āpajjati, saccaṁ bhaṇanto lahukaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.8
Pali: Atthāpatti bhūmigato āpajjati, no vehāsagato. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.9
Pali: Atthāpatti vehāsagato āpajjati, no bhūmigato. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.10
Pali: Atthāpatti nikkhamanto āpajjati, no pavisanto. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.11
Pali: Atthāpatti pavisanto āpajjati, no nikkhamanto. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.12
Pali: Atthāpatti ādiyanto āpajjati, atthāpatti anādiyanto āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.13

pli-tv-pvr7:7.14
Pali: Atthāpatti karonto āpajjati, atthāpatti na karonto āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.15
Pali: Atthāpatti dento āpajjati, atthāpatti na dento āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.16

pli-tv-pvr7:7.17

pli-tv-pvr7:7.18

pli-tv-pvr7:7.19
Pali: Atthāpatti rattiṁ āpajjati, no divā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.20
Pali: Atthāpatti divā āpajjati, no rattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr7:7.21
Pali: Atthāpatti aruṇugge āpajjati, atthāpatti na aruṇugge āpajjati.

pli-tv-pvr7:28.1

Pali: bhaṇḍanakārako hoti kalahakārako vivādakārako bhassakārako saṅghe adhikaraṇakārako, bālo hoti abyatto, āpattibahulo anapadāno gihisaṁsaṭṭho viharati ananulomikehi gihisaṁsaggehi.

pli-tv-pvr7:28.4

pli-tv-pvr7:28.5

pli-tv-pvr7:28.6

pli-tv-pvr7:28.7

pli-tv-pvr7:28.13
Pali: Tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno ākaṅkhamāno saṅgho pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā appaṭinissagge ukkhepanīyakammaṁ kareyya—

pli-tv-pvr7:28.14
Pali: bhaṇḍanakārako hoti …pe… saṅghe adhikaraṇakārako, bālo hoti abyatto, āpattibahulo anapadāno na icchati pāpikaṁ diṭṭhiṁ paṭinissajjituṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr7:29.1
Pali: Tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno ākaṅkhamāno saṅgho āgāḷhāya ceteyya—

pli-tv-pvr7:29.2
Pali: bhaṇḍanakārako hoti kalahakārako vivādakārako bhassakārako saṅghe adhikaraṇakārako, bālo hoti abyatto āpattibahulo anapadāno, gihisaṁsaṭṭho viharati ananulomikehi gihisaṁsaggehi. 

pli-tv-pvr7:29.3
Pali: Tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ kātabbaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr7:29.4
Pali: alajjī ca hoti, bālo ca, apakatatto ca. 

pli-tv-pvr7:29.5
Pali: Aparehipi tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ kātabbaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr7:29.6
Pali: adhisīle sīlavipanno hoti, ajjhācāre ācāravipanno hoti, atidiṭṭhiyā diṭṭhivipanno hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:29.7
Pali: Aparehipi tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ kātabbaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr7:29.8
Pali: kāyikena davena samannāgato hoti, vācasikena davena samannāgato hoti, kāyikavācasikena davena samannāgato hoti.

pli-tv-pvr7:29.10
Pali: kāyikena anācārena samannāgato hoti, vācasikena anācārena samannāgato hoti, kāyikavācasikena anācārena samannāgato hoti.

pli-tv-pvr7:29.14

pli-tv-pvr7:29.16

pli-tv-pvr7:29.17
Pali: Aparehipi tīhaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ kātabbaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr7:29.18
Pali: yāya āpattiyā saṅghena kammaṁ kataṁ hoti taṁ āpattiṁ āpajjati, aññaṁ vā tādisikaṁ, tato vā pāpiṭṭhataraṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr7:29.19

pli-tv-pvr7:29.20

pli-tv-pvr7:33.2
Pali: idamappahāya, yo ca abrahmacārī brahmacāripaṭiñño, yo ca suddhaṁ brahmacāriṁ parisuddhabrahmacariyaṁ carantaṁ amūlakena abrahmacariyena anuddhaṁseti, yo cāyaṁ evaṁvādī evaṁdiṭṭhi—“natthi kāmesu doso”ti so kāmesu pātabyataṁ āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:33.3

pli-tv-pvr7:33.12
Pali: dummaṅkūnaṁ puggalānaṁ niggahāya, pesalānaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ phāsuvihārāya, “mā pāpicchā pakkhaṁ nissāya saṅghaṁ bhindeyyun”ti kulānuddayatāya ca. 

pli-tv-pvr7:33.13
Pali: Tīhi asaddhammehi abhibhūto pariyādinnacitto devadatto āpāyiko nerayiko kappaṭṭho atekiccho pāpicchatā pāpamittatā oramattakena visesādhigamena antarā vosānaṁ āpādi.

Pali: 5. Pañcakavāra 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.1
Pali: Pañca āpattiyo.

Pali: Pañca āpattikkhandhā.

Pali: Pañca vinītavatthūni.

Pali: Pañca puggalā niyatā.

Pali: Pañca chedanakā āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.7
Pali: Pañcahākārehi āpattiṁ āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.8
Pali: Pañca āpattiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.9
Pali: Musāvādapaccayā pañcahākārehi kammaṁ na upeti—

pli-tv-pvr7:63.10
Pali: sayaṁ vā kammaṁ na karoti, paraṁ vā na ajjhesati, chandaṁ vā pārisuddhiṁ vā na deti, kayiramāne kamme paṭikkosati, kate vā pana kamme adhammadiṭṭhi hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.11
Pali: Pañcahākārehi kammaṁ upeti—

pli-tv-pvr7:63.12
Pali: sayaṁ vā kammaṁ karoti, paraṁ vā ajjhesati, chandaṁ vā pārisuddhiṁ vā deti, kayiramāne kamme nappaṭikkosati, kate vā pana kamme dhammadiṭṭhi hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.13
Pali: Pañca piṇḍapātikassa bhikkhuno kappanti—

pli-tv-pvr7:63.14
Pali: anāmantacāro, gaṇabhojanaṁ, paramparabhojanaṁ, anadhiṭṭhānaṁ, avikappanā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.15
Pali: Pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu ussaṅkitaparisaṅkito hoti—

pli-tv-pvr7:63.16
Pali: pāpabhikkhupi akuppadhammopi vesiyāgocaro vā hoti, vidhavāgocaro vā hoti, thullakumārigocaro vā hoti, paṇḍakagocaro vā hoti, bhikkhunigocaro vā hoti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:63.17

pli-tv-pvr7:67.1
Pali: Pañca ādīnavā apāsādike—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.2
Pali: attāpi attānaṁ upavadati, anuviccapi viññū garahanti, pāpako kittisaddo abbhuggacchati, sammūḷho kālaṁ karoti, kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:67.3
Pali: Pañcānisaṁsā pāsādike—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.4
Pali: attāpi attānaṁ na upavadati, anuviccapi viññū pasaṁsanti, kalyāṇo kittisaddo abbhuggacchati, asammūḷho kālaṁ karoti, kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:67.5
Pali: Aparepi pañca ādīnavā apāsādike—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.6
Pali: appasannā na pasīdanti, pasannānaṁ ekaccānaṁ aññathattaṁ hoti, satthusāsanaṁ akataṁ hoti, pacchimā janatā diṭṭhānugatiṁ nāpajjati, cittamassa na pasīdati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:67.7
Pali: Pañcānisaṁsā pāsādike—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.8
Pali: appasannā pasīdanti, pasannānaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya hoti, satthusāsanaṁ kataṁ hoti, pacchimā janatā diṭṭhānugatiṁ āpajjati, cittamassa pasīdati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:67.9
Pali: Pañca ādīnavā kulūpake—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.10
Pali: anāmantacāre āpajjati, raho nisajjāya āpajjati, paṭicchanne āsane āpajjati, mātugāmassa uttarichappañcavācāhi dhammaṁ desento āpajjati, kāmasaṅkappabahulo ca viharati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:67.11
Pali: Pañca ādīnavā kulūpakassa bhikkhuno—

pli-tv-pvr7:67.12
Pali: ativelaṁ kulesu saṁsaṭṭhassa viharato mātugāmassa abhiṇhadassanaṁ, dassane sati saṁsaggo, saṁsagge sati vissāso, vissāse sati otāro, otiṇṇacittassetaṁ bhikkhuno pāṭikaṅkhaṁ anabhirato vā brahmacariyaṁ carissati aññataraṁ vā saṅkiliṭṭhaṁ āpattiṁ āpajjissati sikkhaṁ vā paccakkhāya hīnāyāvattissati. 

pli-tv-pvr7:68.1

pli-tv-pvr7:68.2

pli-tv-pvr7:68.3
Pali: Pañcahi samaṇakappehi phalaṁ paribhuñjitabbaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr7:68.4
Pali: aggiparijitaṁ, satthaparijitaṁ, nakhaparijitaṁ, abījaṁ, nibbattabījaññeva pañcamaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr7:68.6

pli-tv-pvr7:68.8
Pali: nidānaṁ uddisitvā cattāri pārājikāni uddisitvā terasa saṅghādisese uddisitvā avasesaṁ sutena sāvetabbaṁ, ayaṁ tatiyā visuddhi; 

pli-tv-pvr7:68.9
Pali: nidānaṁ uddisitvā cattāri pārājikāni uddisitvā terasa saṅghādisese uddisitvā dve aniyate uddisitvā avasesaṁ sutena sāvetabbaṁ, ayaṁ catutthā visuddhi;

pli-tv-pvr7:68.12

Pali: āpattiṁ jānāti; anāpattiṁ jānāti; lahukaṁ āpattiṁ jānāti; garukaṁ āpattiṁ jānāti; anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussarati, seyyathidaṁ—ekampi jātiṁ dvepi jātiyo tissopi jātiyo catassopi jātiyo pañcapi jātiyo dasapi jātiyo vīsampi jātiyo tiṁsampi jātiyo cattālīsampi jātiyo paññāsampi jātiyo jātisatampi jātisahassampi jātisatasahassampi anekepi saṁvaṭṭakappe anekepi vivaṭṭakappe anekepi saṁvaṭṭavivaṭṭakappe—“amutrāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhappaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto amutra udapādiṁ; tatrāpāsiṁ evaṁnāmo evaṅgotto evaṁvaṇṇo evamāhāro evaṁsukhadukkhappaṭisaṁvedī evamāyupariyanto, so tato cuto idhūpapanno”ti iti sākāraṁ sauddesaṁ anekavihitaṁ pubbenivāsaṁ anussarati; dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passati cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe, sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāti—“ime vata bhonto sattā kāyaduccaritena samannāgatā, vacīduccaritena samannāgatā, manoduccaritena samannāgatā, ariyānaṁ upavādakā, micchādiṭṭhikā, micchādiṭṭhikammasamādānā, te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā apāyaṁ duggatiṁ vinipātaṁ nirayaṁ upapannā, ime vā pana bhonto sattā kāyasucaritena samannāgatā, vacīsucaritena samannāgatā, manosucaritena samannāgatā, ariyānaṁ anupavādakā, sammādiṭṭhikā, sammādiṭṭhikammasamādānā, te kāyassa bhedā paraṁ maraṇā sugatiṁ saggaṁ lokaṁ upapannā”ti iti dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte passati cavamāne upapajjamāne hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāti; āsavānañca khayā anāsavaṁ cetovimuttiṁ paññāvimuttiṁ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṁ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja viharati.

pli-tv-pvr7:113.1

pli-tv-pvr7:126.14
Pali: Dasahaṅgehi samannāgato sāmaṇero nāsetabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr7:127.1
Pali: Dasahaṅgehi samannāgato vinayadharo “bālo” tveva saṅkhaṁ gacchati—

pli-tv-pvr7:127.2
Pali: attano bhāsapariyantaṁ na uggaṇhāti, parassa bhāsapariyantaṁ na uggaṇhāti, attano bhāsapariyantaṁ anuggahetvā parassa bhāsapariyantaṁ anuggahetvā adhammena kāreti, appaṭiññāya āpattiṁ na jānāti, āpattiyā mūlaṁ na jānāti, āpattisamudayaṁ na jānāti, āpattinirodhaṁ na jānāti, āpattinirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ na jānāti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:128.1
Pali: Dasahaṅgehi samannāgato vinayadharo “paṇḍito” tveva saṅkhaṁ gacchati—

pli-tv-pvr7:128.2
Pali: attano bhāsapariyantaṁ uggaṇhāti, parassa bhāsapariyantaṁ uggaṇhāti, attano bhāsapariyantaṁ uggahetvā parassa bhāsapariyantaṁ uggahetvā dhammena kāreti, paṭiññāya āpattiṁ jānāti, āpattiyā mūlaṁ jānāti, āpattisamudayaṁ jānāti, āpattinirodhaṁ jānāti, āpattinirodhagāminiṁ paṭipadaṁ jānāti. 

pli-tv-pvr7:129.1

pli-tv-pvr7:129.2

pli-tv-pvr7:130.2

pli-tv-pvr7:131.2

Pali: Dasahaṅgehi samannāgato vinayadharo “paṇḍito” tveva saṅkhaṁ gacchati—

pli-tv-pvr7:132.2
Pali: ñattiṁ jānāti, ñattiyā karaṇaṁ jānāti, pubbakusalo hoti, aparakusalo hoti, kālaññū ca hoti, āpattānāpattiṁ jānāti, lahukagarukaṁ āpattiṁ jānāti, sāvasesānavasesaṁ āpattiṁ jānāti, duṭṭhullāduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ jānāti, ācariyaparamparā kho panassa suggahitā hoti sumanasikatā sūpadhāritā.

Pali: Aparehipi dasahaṅgehi samannāgato vinayadharo “bālo” tveva saṅkhaṁ gacchati—

pli-tv-pvr7:133.2
Pali: āpattānāpattiṁ na jānāti, lahukagarukaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, sāvasesānavasesaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, duṭṭhullāduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, ubhayāni kho panassa pātimokkhāni vitthārena na svāgatāni honti na suvibhattāni na suppavattīni na suvinicchitāni suttaso anubyañjanaso, āpattānāpattiṁ na jānāti, lahukagarukaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, sāvasesānavasesaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, duṭṭhullāduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, adhikaraṇe ca na vinicchayakusalo hoti.

Pali: Ekādasa cīvarāni na vikappetabbāni.

Pali: Ekādase aruṇuggamane nissaggiyaṁ hoti.

Pali: Ekādasa gaṇṭhikā kappiyā.

Pali: Ekādasa pathavī kappiyā.

Pali: Ekādasa nissayapaṭippassaddhiyo. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.15
Pali: Ekādasa puggalā avandiyā.

Pali: Ekādasa paramāni. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.17
Pali: Ekādasa varāni yāciṁsu. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.18
Pali: Ekādasa sīmādosā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.19
Pali: Akkosakaparibhāsake puggale ekādasādīnavā pāṭikaṅkhā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.20
Pali: Mettāya cetovimuttiyā āsevitāya bhāvitāya bahulīkatāya yānīkatāya vatthukatāya anuṭṭhitāya paricitāya susamāraddhāya ekādasānisaṁsā pāṭikaṅkhā. 

pli-tv-pvr7:144.21
Pali: Sukhaṁ supati, sukhaṁ paṭibujjhati, na pāpakaṁ supinaṁ passati, manussānaṁ piyo hoti, amanussānaṁ piyo hoti, devatā rakkhanti, nāssa aggi vā visaṁ vā satthaṁ vā kamati, tuvaṭṭaṁ cittaṁ samādhiyati, mukhavaṇṇo vippasīdati, asammūḷho kālaṁ karoti, uttari appaṭivijjhanto brahmalokūpago hoti—

pli-tv-pvr7:144.22
Pali: mettāya cetovimuttiyā āsevitāya bhāvitāya bahulīkatāya yānīkatāya vatthukatāya anuṭṭhitāya paricitāya susamāraddhāya ime ekādasānisaṁsā pāṭikaṅkhāti.

Pali: Parivāra 

pli-tv-pvr9:0.2
Pali: 9. Atthavasapakaraṇa 

pli-tv-pvr9:1.1
Pali: Dasa atthavase paṭicca tathāgatena sāvakānaṁ sikkhāpadaṁ paññattaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr9:1.2
Pali: saṅghasuṭṭhutāya, saṅghaphāsutāya, dummaṅkūnaṁ puggalānaṁ niggahāya, pesalānaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ phāsuvihārāya, diṭṭhadhammikānaṁ āsavānaṁ saṁvarāya, samparāyikānaṁ āsavānaṁ paṭighātāya, appasannānaṁ pasādāya, pasannānaṁ bhiyyobhāvāya, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā vinayānuggahāya. 

pli-tv-pvr9:2.1

Pali: Cattāri adhikaraṇāni.

Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, kiccādhikaraṇaṁ—

Pali: imāni cattāri adhikaraṇāni. 

pli-tv-pvr11:2.1
Pali: Imesaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ kati ukkoṭā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:2.2

pli-tv-pvr11:2.3
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇassa dve ukkoṭā, anuvādādhikaraṇassa cattāro ukkoṭā, āpattādhikaraṇassa tayo ukkoṭā, kiccādhikaraṇassa eko ukkoṭo—

pli-tv-pvr11:2.4
Pali: imesaṁ catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ ime dasa ukkoṭā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:3.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭento kati samathe ukkoṭeti?

pli-tv-pvr11:3.3
