Pali: Katihākārehi ukkoṭanaṁ pasavati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:5.3
Pali: Katihaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:5.4
Pali: Kati puggalā adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭentā āpattiṁ āpajjanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:6.1
Pali: Dvādasa ukkoṭā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:6.2
Pali: Dasahākārehi ukkoṭanaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:6.3
Pali: Catūhaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:6.4
Pali: Cattāro puggalā adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭentā āpattiṁ āpajjanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:7.1
Pali: Katame dvādasa ukkoṭā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:7.2
Pali: Akataṁ kammaṁ, dukkaṭaṁ kammaṁ, puna kātabbaṁ kammaṁ, anihataṁ, dunnihataṁ, puna nihanitabbaṁ, avinicchitaṁ, duvinicchitaṁ, puna vinicchitabbaṁ, avūpasantaṁ, duvūpasantaṁ, puna vūpasametabbanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:7.3
Pali: ime dvādasa ukkoṭā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:8.1
Pali: Katamehi dasahākārehi ukkoṭanaṁ pasavati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:8.2
Pali: Tattha jātakaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, tattha jātakaṁ vūpasantaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, antarāmagge adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, antarāmagge vūpasantaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, tattha gataṁ adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, tattha gataṁ vūpasantaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, sativinayaṁ ukkoṭeti, amūḷhavinayaṁ ukkoṭeti, tassapāpiyasikaṁ ukkoṭeti, tiṇavatthārakaṁ ukkoṭeti—

pli-tv-pvr11:8.3
Pali: imehi dasahākārehi ukkoṭanaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:9.1
Pali: Katamehi catūhaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:9.2
Pali: Chandāgatiṁ gacchanto adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, dosāgatiṁ gacchanto adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, mohāgatiṁ gacchanto adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti, bhayāgatiṁ gacchanto adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti—

pli-tv-pvr11:9.3
Pali: imehi catūhaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭeti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:10.1
Pali: Katame cattāro puggalā adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭentā āpattiṁ āpajjanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:10.2
Pali: Tadahupasampanno ukkoṭeti ukkoṭanakaṁ pācittiyaṁ, āgantuko ukkoṭeti ukkoṭanakaṁ pācittiyaṁ, kārako ukkoṭeti ukkoṭanakaṁ pācittiyaṁ, chandadāyako ukkoṭeti ukkoṭanakaṁ pācittiyaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr11:10.3
Pali: ime cattāro puggalā adhikaraṇaṁ ukkoṭentā āpattiṁ āpajjanti.

pli-tv-pvr11:11.1

pli-tv-pvr11:11.2

pli-tv-pvr11:17.0
Pali: 3. Adhikaraṇamūlādi 

pli-tv-pvr11:17.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ kati mūlāni, kati samuṭṭhānā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:17.2
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ tettiṁsa mūlāni, tettiṁsa samuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:18.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamāni tettiṁsa mūlāni? 

pli-tv-pvr11:18.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇassa dvādasa mūlāni, anuvādādhikaraṇassa cuddasa mūlāni, āpattādhikaraṇassa cha mūlāni, kiccādhikaraṇassa ekaṁ mūlaṁ, saṅgho—

pli-tv-pvr11:18.3
Pali: catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ imāni tettiṁsa mūlāni. 

pli-tv-pvr11:19.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katame tettiṁsa samuṭṭhānā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:19.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇassa aṭṭhārasabhedakaravatthūni samuṭṭhānā, anuvādādhikaraṇassa catasso vipattiyo samuṭṭhānā, āpattādhikaraṇassa sattāpattikkhandhā samuṭṭhānā, kiccādhikaraṇassa cattāri kammāni samuṭṭhānā—

pli-tv-pvr11:19.3
Pali: catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ ime tettiṁsa samuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.0
Pali: 4. Adhikaraṇapaccayāpatti 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ āpattānāpattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ na āpatti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.3
Pali: Kiṁ pana vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.4
Pali: Āma, vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyya. 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.5
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.6
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.7
Pali: Upasampannaṁ omasati, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:20.8
Pali: anupasampannaṁ omasati, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr11:20.9
Pali: vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā imā dve āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:21.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:21.2
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:21.3
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:21.4
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:21.5
Pali: Katihi adhikaraṇehi, katisu ṭhānesu, katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ ekaṁ vipattiṁ bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:22.2
Pali: ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.3
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.4
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ dvīhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr11:22.5
Pali: siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.6
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.7
Pali: Ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:22.8
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.9
Pali: tīsu ṭhānesu—

pli-tv-pvr11:22.10
Pali: saṅghamajjhe, gaṇamajjhe, puggalassa santike; 

pli-tv-pvr11:22.11
Pali: tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:22.12
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ āpattānāpattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.2
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ na āpatti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.3
Pali: Kiṁ pana anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.4
Pali: Āma, anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyya. 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.5
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā, kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.6
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā tisso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.7
Pali: Bhikkhuṁ amūlakena pārājikena dhammena anuddhaṁseti, āpatti saṅghādisesassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.8
Pali: amūlakena saṅghādisesena anuddhaṁseti, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:23.9
Pali: amūlikāya ācāravipattiyā anuddhaṁseti, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr11:23.10
Pali: anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā imā tisso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:24.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:24.2
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:24.3
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:24.4
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:24.5
Pali: Katihi adhikaraṇehi, katisu ṭhānesu, katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.2
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ, siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.3
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.4
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ tīhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.5
Pali: siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.6
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ tīhi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.7
Pali: Yā tā āpattiyo garukā tā āpattiyo ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.8
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.9
Pali: ekamhi ṭhāne—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.10
Pali: saṅghamajjhe; 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.11
Pali: dvīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.12
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.13
Pali: Yā tā āpattiyo lahukā tā āpattiyo ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.14
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.15
Pali: tīsu ṭhānesu—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.16
Pali: saṅghamajjhe gaṇamajjhe puggalassa santike; 

pli-tv-pvr11:25.17
Pali: tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:25.18
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ āpattānāpattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.2
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ āpatti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.3
Pali: Kiṁ pana āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.4
Pali: Āma, āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyya. 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.5
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.6
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.7
Pali: Bhikkhunī jānaṁ pārājikaṁ dhammaṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.8
Pali: vematikā paṭicchādeti, āpatti thullaccayassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.9
Pali: bhikkhu saṅghādisesaṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti pācittiyassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:26.10
Pali: ācāravipattiṁ paṭicchādeti, āpatti dukkaṭassa—

pli-tv-pvr11:26.11
Pali: āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā imā catasso āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:27.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:27.2
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:27.3
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:27.4
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:27.5
Pali: Katihi adhikaraṇehi, katisu ṭhānesu, katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.2
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.3
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.4
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ catūhi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.5
Pali: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.6
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.7
Pali: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.8
Pali: Yā sā āpatti anavasesā sā āpatti na katamena adhikaraṇena, na katamamhi ṭhāne, na katamena samathena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.9
Pali: Yā tā āpattiyo lahukā tā āpattiyo ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.10
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.11
Pali: tīsu ṭhānesu—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.12
Pali: saṅghamajjhe, gaṇamajjhe, puggalassa santike; 

pli-tv-pvr11:28.13
Pali: tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:28.14
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ āpattānāpattīti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.2
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ na āpatti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.3
Pali: Kiṁ pana kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyyāti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.4
Pali: Āma, kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā āpattiṁ āpajjeyya. 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.5
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā kati āpattiyo āpajjati? 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.6
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.7
Pali: Ukkhittānuvattikā bhikkhunī yāvatatiyaṁ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjati, ñattiyā dukkaṭaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.8
Pali: dvīhi kammavācāhi thullaccayā; 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.9
Pali: kammavācāpariyosāne āpatti pārājikassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.10
Pali: bhedakānuvattakā bhikkhū yāvatatiyaṁ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjanti, āpatti saṅghādisesassa; 

pli-tv-pvr11:29.11
Pali: pāpikāya diṭṭhiyā yāvatatiyaṁ samanubhāsanāya na paṭinissajjanti, āpatti pācittiyassa—

pli-tv-pvr11:29.12
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā imā pañca āpattiyo āpajjati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:30.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ kati vipattiyo bhajanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:30.2
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ katamaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:30.3
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ katihi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:30.4
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ katihi samuṭṭhānehi samuṭṭhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:30.5
Pali: Katihi adhikaraṇehi, katisu ṭhānesu, katihi samathehi sammanti? 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.1
Pali: Tā āpattiyo catunnaṁ vipattīnaṁ dve vipattiyo bhajanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.2
Pali: siyā sīlavipattiṁ siyā ācāravipattiṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.3
Pali: Catunnaṁ adhikaraṇānaṁ āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.4
Pali: Sattannaṁ āpattikkhandhānaṁ pañcahi āpattikkhandhehi saṅgahitā—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.5
Pali: siyā pārājikāpattikkhandhena, siyā saṅghādisesāpattikkhandhena, siyā thullaccayāpattikkhandhena, siyā pācittiyāpattikkhandhena, siyā dukkaṭāpattikkhandhena. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.6
Pali: Channaṁ āpattisamuṭṭhānānaṁ ekena samuṭṭhānena samuṭṭhanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.7
Pali: kāyato ca vācato ca cittato ca samuṭṭhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.8
Pali: Yā sā āpatti anavasesā sā āpatti na katamena adhikaraṇena, na katamamhi ṭhāne, na katamena samathena sammati. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.9
Pali: Yā sā āpatti garukā sā āpatti ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.10
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.11
Pali: ekamhi ṭhāne—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.12
Pali: saṅghamajjhe; 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.13
Pali: dvīhi samathehi sammati—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.14
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.15
Pali: Yā tā āpattiyo lahukā tā āpattiyo ekena adhikaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.16
Pali: kiccādhikaraṇena; 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.17
Pali: tīsu ṭhānesu—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.18
Pali: saṅghamajjhe, gaṇamajjhe, puggalassa santike; 

pli-tv-pvr11:31.19
Pali: tīhi samathehi sammanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:31.20
Pali: siyā sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca, siyā sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.0
Pali: 5. Adhikaraṇādhippāya 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.1
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.2
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇaṁ na hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.3
Pali: api ca, vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.5
Pali: Idha bhikkhū vivadanti—

pli-tv-pvr11:32.6
Pali: dhammoti vā adhammoti vā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.7
Pali: duṭṭhullāpattīti vā aduṭṭhullāpattīti vā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.8
Pali: Yaṁ tattha bhaṇḍanaṁ kalaho viggaho vivādo nānāvādo aññathāvādo vipaccatāya vohāro medhakaṁ, idaṁ vuccati vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.9
Pali: Vivādādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.10
Pali: Vivadamāno anuvadati anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.11
Pali: Anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.12
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:32.13
Pali: Evaṁ vivādādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.1
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.2
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ na hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.3
Pali: api ca anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.5
Pali: Idha bhikkhū bhikkhuṁ anuvadanti sīlavipattiyā vā ācāravipattiyā vā diṭṭhivipattiyā vā ājīvavipattiyā vā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.6
Pali: Yo tattha anuvādo anuvadanā anullapanā anubhaṇanā anusampavaṅkatā abbhussahanatā anubalappadānaṁ, idaṁ vuccati anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.7
Pali: Anuvādādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati, vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.8
Pali: Vivadamāno anuvadati, anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.9
Pali: Anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.10
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti, kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:33.11
Pali: Evaṁ anuvādādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.1
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.2
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇaṁ na hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.3
Pali: api ca āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.5
Pali: Pañcapi āpattikkhandhā āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, sattapi āpattikkhandhā āpattādhikaraṇaṁ, idaṁ vuccati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.6
Pali: Āpattādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.7
Pali: Vivadamāno anuvadati anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.8
Pali: Anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.9
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:34.10
Pali: Evaṁ āpattādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.1
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.2
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇaṁ na hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, na hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.3
Pali: api ca kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.4
Pali: Yathā kathaṁ viya? 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.5
Pali: Yā saṅghassa kiccayatā karaṇīyatā apalokanakammaṁ ñattikammaṁ ñattidutiyakammaṁ ñatticatutthakammaṁ, idaṁ vuccati kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.6
Pali: Kiccādhikaraṇe saṅgho vivadati vivādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.7
Pali: Vivadamāno anuvadati anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.8
Pali: Anuvadamāno āpattiṁ āpajjati āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.9
Pali: Tāya āpattiyā saṅgho kammaṁ karoti kiccādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:35.10
Pali: Evaṁ kiccādhikaraṇapaccayā hoti vivādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ, hoti āpattādhikaraṇaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.0
Pali: 6. Pucchāvāra 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.1
Pali: Yattha sativinayo tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.2
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha sativinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.3
Pali: Yattha amūḷhavinayo tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.4
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha amūḷhavinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.5
Pali: Yattha paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.6
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.7
Pali: Yattha yebhuyyasikā tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.8
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha yebhuyyasikā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.9
Pali: Yattha tassapāpiyasikā tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.10
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha tassapāpiyasikā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.11
Pali: Yattha tiṇavatthārako tattha sammukhāvinayo? 

pli-tv-pvr11:36.12
Pali: Yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha tiṇavatthārako? 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.0
Pali: 7. Vissajjanāvāra 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.1
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca sativinayena ca adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasammati—

pli-tv-pvr11:37.2
Pali: yattha sativinayo tattha sammukhāvinayo, yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha sativinayo, na tattha amūḷhavinayo, na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, na tattha yebhuyyasikā, na tattha tassapāpiyasikā, na tattha tiṇavatthārako. 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.3
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye sammukhāvinayena ca amūḷhavinayena ca …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca paṭiññātakaraṇena ca …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.5
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca yebhuyyasikāya ca …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.6
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca tassapāpiyasikāya ca …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:37.7
Pali: sammukhāvinayena ca tiṇavatthārakena ca adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasammati—

pli-tv-pvr11:37.8
Pali: yattha tiṇavatthārako tattha sammukhāvinayo, yattha sammukhāvinayo tattha tiṇavatthārako, na tattha sativinayo, na tattha amūḷhavinayo, na tattha paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ, na tattha yebhuyyasikā, na tattha tassapāpiyasikā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.0
Pali: 8. Saṁsaṭṭhavāra 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayoti vā sativinayoti vā ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā udāhu visaṁsaṭṭhā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.2
Pali: Labbhā ca panimesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetuṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.3
Pali: Sammukhāvinayoti vā amūḷhavinayoti vā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.4
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā paṭiññātakaraṇanti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.5
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā yebhuyyasikāti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.6
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā tassapāpiyasikāti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.7
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā tiṇavatthārakoti vā—ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā, udāhu visaṁsaṭṭhā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:38.8
Pali: Labbhā ca panimesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetuṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayoti vā sativinayoti vā—

pli-tv-pvr11:39.2
Pali: ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā, no visaṁsaṭṭhā; 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.3
Pali: na ca labbhā imesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetuṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.4
Pali: Sammukhāvinayoti vā amūḷhavinayoti vā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.5
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā paṭiññātakaraṇanti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.6
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā yebhuyyasikāti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.7
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā tassapāpiyasikāti vā … 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.8
Pali: sammukhāvinayoti vā tiṇavatthārakoti vā—

pli-tv-pvr11:39.9
Pali: ime dhammā saṁsaṭṭhā, no visaṁsaṭṭhā; 

pli-tv-pvr11:39.10
Pali: na ca labbhā imesaṁ dhammānaṁ vinibbhujitvā vinibbhujitvā nānākaraṇaṁ paññāpetuṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.0
Pali: 9. Sattasamathanidāna 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.2
Pali: Sativinayo kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro, kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.3
Pali: Amūḷhavinayo kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro, kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.4
Pali: Paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ kiṁnidānaṁ, kiṁsamudayaṁ, kiṁjātikaṁ, kiṁpabhavaṁ, kiṁsambhāraṁ, kiṁsamuṭṭhānaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.5
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā kiṁnidānā, kiṁsamudayā, kiṁjātikā, kiṁpabhavā, kiṁsambhārā, kiṁsamuṭṭhānā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.6
Pali: Tassapāpiyasikā kiṁnidānā, kiṁsamudayā, kiṁjātikā, kiṁpabhavā, kiṁsambhārā, kiṁsamuṭṭhānā? 

pli-tv-pvr11:40.7
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro, kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo nidānanidāno, nidānasamudayo, nidānajātiko, nidānapabhavo, nidānasambhāro, nidānasamuṭṭhāno. 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.2
Pali: Sativinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.3
Pali: amūḷhavinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.4
Pali: paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ nidānanidānaṁ, nidānasamudayaṁ, nidānajātikaṁ, nidānapabhavaṁ, nidānasambhāraṁ, nidānasamuṭṭhānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.5
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.6
Pali: tassapāpiyasikā nidānanidānā, nidānasamudayā, nidānajātikā, nidānapabhavā, nidānasambhārā, nidānasamuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:41.7
Pali: Tiṇavatthārako nidānanidāno, nidānasamudayo, nidānajātiko, nidānapabhavo, nidānasambhāro, nidānasamuṭṭhāno. 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro, kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.2
Pali: Sativinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.3
Pali: amūḷhavinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.4
Pali: paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.5
Pali: yebhuyyasikā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.6
Pali: tassapāpiyasikā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:42.7
Pali: tiṇavatthārako kiṁnidāno, kiṁsamudayo, kiṁjātiko, kiṁpabhavo, kiṁsambhāro, kiṁsamuṭṭhāno? 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.1
Pali: Sammukhāvinayo hetunidāno, hetusamudayo, hetujātiko, hetupabhavo, hetusambhāro, hetusamuṭṭhāno. 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.2
Pali: Sativinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.3
Pali: amūḷhavinayo …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.4
Pali: paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ hetunidānaṁ, hetusamudayaṁ, hetujātikaṁ, hetupabhavaṁ, hetusambhāraṁ, hetusamuṭṭhānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.5
Pali: Yebhuyyasikā …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.6
Pali: tassapāpiyasikā hetunidānā, hetusamudayā, hetujātikā, hetupabhavā, hetusambhārā, hetusamuṭṭhānā. 

pli-tv-pvr11:43.7

Pali: Aññañca tāhaṁ pucchāmi, 

pli-tv-pvr12:16.4
Pali: Kīdiso vuccati bālacodako. 

pli-tv-pvr12:17.1
Pali: Pubbāparaṁ na jānāti, 

pli-tv-pvr12:17.2

pli-tv-pvr12:17.4
Pali: Anusandhivacanapathassa akovido; 

pli-tv-pvr12:17.5

pli-tv-pvr12:22.1
Pali: Aparaṁ gāthāsaṅgaṇikaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr13:28.1
Pali: Codanā anuvijjā ca, 

pli-tv-pvr13:28.2
Pali: ādi mūlenuposatho; 

pli-tv-pvr13:28.3
Pali: Gati codanakaṇḍamhi, 

pli-tv-pvr13:28.4
Pali: sāsanaṁ patiṭṭhāpayanti.

Pali: 14. Anuvijjakassapaṭipatti 

pli-tv-pvr14:1.1
Pali: Saṅgāmāvacarena bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamantena: 

pli-tv-pvr14:1.2
Pali: nīcacittena saṅgho upasaṅkamitabbo; 

pli-tv-pvr14:1.3
Pali: rajoharaṇasamena cittena; 

pli-tv-pvr14:1.4
Pali: āsanakusalena bhavitabbaṁ nisajjakusalena; there bhikkhū anupakhajjantena, nave bhikkhū āsanena appaṭibāhantena, yathāpatirūpe āsane nisīditabbaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr14:1.5
Pali: anānākathikena bhavitabbaṁ atiracchānakathikena; sāmaṁ vā dhammo bhāsitabbo paro vā ajjhesitabbo ariyo vā tuṇhībhāvo nātimaññitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr14:2.1
Pali: Saṅghena anumatena puggalena anuvijjakena anuvijjitukāmena na upajjhāyo pucchitabbo, na ācariyo pucchitabbo, na saddhivihāriko pucchitabbo, na antevāsiko pucchitabbo, na samānupajjhāyako pucchitabbo, na samānācariyako pucchitabbo, na jāti pucchitabbā, na nāmaṁ pucchitabbaṁ, na gottaṁ pucchitabbaṁ, na āgamo pucchitabbo, na kulapadeso pucchitabbo, na jātibhūmi pucchitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr14:2.2
Pali: Taṁ kiṁ kāraṇā? 

pli-tv-pvr14:2.3
Pali: Atrassa pemaṁ vā doso vā. 

pli-tv-pvr14:2.4
Pali: Peme vā sati dose vā, chandāpi gaccheyya, dosāpi gaccheyya, mohāpi gaccheyya, bhayāpi gaccheyya. 

pli-tv-pvr14:3.1
Pali: Saṅghena anumatena puggalena anuvijjakena anuvijjitukāmena saṅghagarukena bhavitabbaṁ no puggalagarukena, saddhammagarukena bhavitabbaṁ no āmisagarukena, atthavasikena bhavitabbaṁ no parisakappikena, kālena anuvijjitabbaṁ no akālena, bhūtena anuvijjitabbaṁ no abhūtena, saṇhena anuvijjitabbaṁ no pharusena, atthasaṁhitena anuvijjitabbaṁ no anatthasaṁhitena, mettācittena anuvijjitabbaṁ no dosantarena, na upakaṇṇakajappinā bhavitabbaṁ, na jimhaṁ pekkhitabbaṁ, na akkhi nikhaṇitabbaṁ, na bhamukaṁ ukkhipitabbaṁ, na sīsaṁ ukkhipitabbaṁ, na hatthavikāro kātabbo, na hatthamuddā dassetabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr14:4.1
Pali: Āsanakusalena bhavitabbaṁ nisajjakusalena, yugamattaṁ pekkhantena atthaṁ anuvidhiyantena sake āsane nisīditabbaṁ, na ca āsanā vuṭṭhātabbaṁ, na vītihātabbaṁ, na kummaggo sevitabbo, na bāhāvikkhepakaṁ bhaṇitabbaṁ, aturitena bhavitabbaṁ asāhasikena, acaṇḍikatena bhavitabbaṁ vacanakkhamena, mettācittena bhavitabbaṁ hitānukampinā, kāruṇikena bhavitabbaṁ hitaparisakkinā, asamphappalāpinā bhavitabbaṁ pariyantabhāṇinā, averavasikena bhavitabbaṁ anasuruttena, attā pariggahetabbo, paro pariggahetabbo, codako pariggahetabbo, cuditako pariggahetabbo, adhammacodako pariggahetabbo, adhammacuditako pariggahetabbo, dhammacodako pariggahetabbo, dhammacuditako pariggahetabbo, vuttaṁ ahāpentena avuttaṁ apakāsentena otiṇṇāni padabyañjanāni sādhukaṁ pariggahetvā paro paṭipucchitvā yathā paṭiññāya kāretabbo, mando hāsetabbo, bhīrū assāsetabbo, caṇḍo nisedhetabbo, asuci vibhāvetabbo, ujumaddavena na chandāgatiṁ gantabbaṁ, na dosāgatiṁ gantabbaṁ, na mohāgatiṁ gantabbaṁ, na bhayāgatiṁ gantabbaṁ, majjhattena bhavitabbaṁ dhammesu ca puggalesu ca. 

pli-tv-pvr14:4.2
Pali: Evañca pana anuvijjako anuvijjamāno satthu ceva sāsanakaro hoti, viññūnañca sabrahmacārīnaṁ piyo ca hoti manāpo ca garu ca bhāvanīyo ca. 

pli-tv-pvr14:5.1
Pali: Suttaṁ saṁsandanatthāya, opammaṁ nidassanatthāya, attho viññāpanatthāya, paṭipucchā ṭhapanatthāya, okāsakammaṁ codanatthāya, codanā sāraṇatthāya, sāraṇā savacanīyatthāya, savacanīyaṁ palibodhatthāya, palibodho vinicchayatthāya, vinicchayo santīraṇatthāya, santīraṇaṁ ṭhānāṭhānagamanatthāya, ṭhānāṭhānagamanaṁ dummaṅkūnaṁ puggalānaṁ niggahatthāya, pesalānaṁ bhikkhūnaṁ sampaggahatthāya, saṅgho sampariggahasampaṭicchanatthāya, saṅghena anumatā puggalā paccekaṭṭhāyino avisaṁvādakaṭṭhāyino. 

pli-tv-pvr14:6.1
Pali: Vinayo saṁvaratthāya, saṁvaro avippaṭisāratthāya, avippaṭisāro pāmujjatthāya, pāmujjaṁ pītatthāya, pīti passaddhatthāya, passaddhi sukhatthāya, sukhaṁ samādhatthāya, samādhi yathābhūtañāṇadassanatthāya, yathābhūtañāṇadassanaṁ nibbidatthāya, nibbidā virāgatthāya, virāgo vimuttatthāya, vimutti vimuttiñāṇadassanatthāya, vimuttiñāṇadassanaṁ anupādāparinibbānatthāya. 

pli-tv-pvr14:6.2

pli-tv-pvr14:6.3
Pali: yadidaṁ anupādācittassa vimokkhoti. 

pli-tv-pvr14:7.1

pli-tv-pvr15:0.3
Pali: 1. Voharantenajānitabbādi 

pli-tv-pvr15:1.1
Pali: Saṅgāmāvacarena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharantena vatthu jānitabbaṁ, vipatti jānitabbā, āpatti jānitabbā, nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, ākāro jānitabbo, pubbāparaṁ jānitabbaṁ, katākataṁ jānitabbaṁ, kammaṁ jānitabbaṁ, adhikaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ, samatho jānitabbo, na chandāgati gantabbā, na dosāgati gantabbā, na mohāgati gantabbā, na bhayāgati gantabbā, saññāpanīye ṭhāne saññāpetabbaṁ, nijjhāpanīye ṭhāne nijjhāpetabbaṁ, pekkhanīye ṭhāne pekkhitabbaṁ, pasādanīye ṭhāne pasādetabbaṁ, “laddhapakkhomhī”ti parapakkho nāvajānitabbo, bahussutomhīti appassuto nāvajānitabbo, therataromhīti navakataro nāvajānitabbo, asampattaṁ na byāhātabbaṁ, sampattaṁ dhammato vinayato na parihāpetabbaṁ, yena dhammena yena vinayena yena satthusāsanena taṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasammati, tathā taṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasametabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:2.1
Pali: Vatthu jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:2.2
Pali: aṭṭhapārājikānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, tevīsasaṅghādisesānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, dveaniyatānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, dvecattārīsanissaggiyānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, aṭṭhāsītisatapācittiyānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, dvādasapāṭidesanīyānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, dukkaṭānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ, dubbhāsitānaṁ vatthu jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:3.1
Pali: Vipatti jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:3.2
Pali: sīlavipatti jānitabbā, ācāravipatti jānitabbā, diṭṭhivipatti jānitabbā, ājīvavipatti jānitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:4.1
Pali: Āpatti jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:4.2
Pali: pārājikāpatti jānitabbā, saṅghādisesāpatti jānitabbā, thullaccayāpatti jānitabbā, pācittiyāpatti jānitabbā, pāṭidesanīyāpatti jānitabbā, dukkaṭāpatti jānitabbā, dubbhāsitāpatti jānitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:5.1
Pali: Nidānaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:5.2
Pali: aṭṭhapārājikānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, tevīsasaṅghādisesānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, dveaniyatānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, dvecattārīsanissaggiyānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, aṭṭhāsītisatapācittiyānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, dvādasapāṭidesanīyānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, dukkaṭānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ, dubbhāsitānaṁ nidānaṁ jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.1
Pali: Ākāro jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.2
Pali: saṅgho ākārato jānitabbo, gaṇo ākārato jānitabbo, puggalo ākārato jānitabbo, codako ākārato jānitabbo, cuditako ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.3
Pali: Saṅgho ākārato jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.4
Pali: paṭibalo nu kho ayaṁ saṅgho imaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasametuṁ dhammena vinayena satthusāsanena udāhu noti, evaṁ saṅgho ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.5
Pali: Gaṇo ākārato jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.6
Pali: paṭibalo nu kho ayaṁ gaṇo imaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasametuṁ dhammena vinayena satthusāsanena udāhu noti, evaṁ gaṇo ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.7
Pali: Puggalo ākārato jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.8
Pali: paṭibalo nu kho ayaṁ puggalo imaṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasametuṁ dhammena vinayena satthusāsanena udāhu noti, evaṁ puggalo ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.9
Pali: Codako ākārato jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.10
Pali: kacci nu kho ayamāyasmā pañcasu dhammesu patiṭṭhāya paraṁ codeti udāhu noti, evaṁ codako ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.11
Pali: Cuditako ākārato jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:6.12
Pali: kacci nu kho ayamāyasmā dvīsu dhammesu patiṭṭhito sacce ca akuppe ca udāhu noti, evaṁ cuditako ākārato jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:7.1
Pali: Pubbāparaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:7.2
Pali: kacci nu kho ayamāyasmā vatthuto vā vatthuṁ saṅkamati, vipattito vā vipattiṁ saṅkamati, āpattito vā āpattiṁ saṅkamati, avajānitvā vā paṭijānāti, paṭijānitvā vā avajānāti, aññena vā aññaṁ paṭicarati, udāhu noti, evaṁ pubbāparaṁ jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.1
Pali: Katākataṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.2
Pali: methunadhammo jānitabbo, methunadhammassa anulomaṁ jānitabbaṁ, methunadhammassa pubbabhāgo jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.3
Pali: Methunadhammo jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.4
Pali: dvayaṁdvayasamāpatti jānitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.5
Pali: Methunadhammassa anulomaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.6
Pali: bhikkhu attano mukhena parassa aṅgajātaṁ gaṇhāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.7
Pali: Methunadhammassa pubbabhāgo jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:8.8
Pali: vaṇṇāvaṇṇo, kāyasaṁsaggo, duṭṭhullavācā, attakāmapāricariyā, vacanamanuppadānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:9.1
Pali: Kammaṁ jānitabbanti

Pali: soḷasakammāni jānitabbāni—

pli-tv-pvr15:9.3

pli-tv-pvr15:10.3
Pali: vivādādhikaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ, anuvādādhikaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ, āpattādhikaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ, kiccādhikaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:11.1
Pali: Samatho jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr15:11.2
Pali: satta samathā jānitabbā—

pli-tv-pvr15:11.3
Pali: sammukhāvinayo jānitabbo, sativinayo jānitabbo, amūḷhavinayo jānitabbo, paṭiññātakaraṇaṁ jānitabbaṁ, yebhuyyasikā jānitabbā, tassapāpiyasikā jānitabbā, tiṇavatthārako jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.0
Pali: 2. Agatiagantabba 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.1
Pali: Na chandāgati gantabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.2
Pali: chandāgatiṁ gacchanto kathaṁ chandāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.3
Pali: Idhekacco—“ayaṁ me upajjhāyo vā ācariyo vā saddhivihāriko vā antevāsiko vā samānupajjhāyako vā samānācariyako vā sandiṭṭho vā sambhatto vā ñātisālohito vā”ti, tassānukampāya tassānurakkhāya adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti, avinayaṁ vinayoti dīpeti, vinayaṁ avinayoti dīpeti, abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatena bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatena abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, apaññattaṁ tathāgatena paññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, paññattaṁ tathāgatena apaññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, anāpattiṁ āpattīti dīpeti, āpattiṁ anāpattīti dīpeti, lahukaṁ āpattiṁ garukā āpattīti dīpeti, garukaṁ āpattiṁ lahukā āpattīti dīpeti, sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ anavasesā āpattīti dīpeti, anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ sāvasesā āpattīti dīpeti, duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.4
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi chandāgatiṁ gacchanto bahujanāhitāya paṭipanno hoti bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.5
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi chandāgatiṁ gacchanto khataṁ upahataṁ attānaṁ pariharati, sāvajjo ca hoti sānuvajjo ca viññūnaṁ, bahuñca apuññaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:12.6
Pali: Chandāgatiṁ gacchanto evaṁ chandāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.1
Pali: Na dosāgati gantabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.2
Pali: dosāgatiṁ gacchanto kathaṁ dosāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.3
Pali: Idhekacco anatthaṁ me acarīti āghātaṁ bandhati, anatthaṁ me caratīti āghātaṁ bandhati, anatthaṁ me carissatīti āghātaṁ bandhati, piyassa me manāpassa anatthaṁ acari … anatthaṁ carati … anatthaṁ carissatīti āghātaṁ bandhati, appiyassa me amanāpassa atthaṁ acari … atthaṁ carati … atthaṁ carissatīti āghātaṁ bandhati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.4
Pali: Imehi navahi āghātavatthūhi āghāto paṭighāto kuddho kodhābhibhūto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.5
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.6
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi dosāgatiṁ gacchanto bahujanāhitāya paṭipanno hoti bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.7
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi dosāgatiṁ gacchanto khataṁ upahataṁ attānaṁ pariharati, sāvajjo ca hoti sānuvajjo ca viññūnaṁ bahuñca apuññaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:13.8
Pali: Dosāgatiṁ gacchanto evaṁ dosāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.1
Pali: Na mohāgati gantabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.2
Pali: mohāgatiṁ gacchanto kathaṁ mohāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.3
Pali: Ratto rāgavasena gacchati, duṭṭho dosavasena gacchati, mūḷho mohavasena gacchati, parāmaṭṭho diṭṭhivasena gacchati, mūḷho sammūḷho mohābhibhūto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.4
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.5
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi mohāgatiṁ gacchanto bahujanāhitāya paṭipanno hoti bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.6
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi mohāgatiṁ gacchanto khataṁ upahataṁ attānaṁ pariharati, sāvajjo ca hoti sānuvajjo ca viññūnaṁ, bahuñca apuññaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:14.7
Pali: Mohāgatiṁ gacchanto evaṁ mohāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.1
Pali: Na bhayāgati gantabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.2
Pali: bhayāgatiṁ gacchanto kathaṁ bhayāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.3
Pali: Idhekacco—“ayaṁ visamanissito vā gahananissito vā balavanissito vā kakkhaḷo pharuso jīvitantarāyaṁ vā brahmacariyantarāyaṁ vā karissatī”ti, tassa bhayā bhīto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti, avinayaṁ vinayoti dīpeti, vinayaṁ avinayoti dīpeti, abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatena bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatena abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, apaññattaṁ tathāgatena paññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, paññattaṁ tathāgatena apaññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpeti, anāpattiṁ āpattīti dīpeti, āpattiṁ anāpattīti dīpeti, lahukaṁ āpattiṁ garukā āpattīti dīpeti, garukaṁ āpattiṁ lahukā āpattīti dīpeti, sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ anavasesā āpattīti dīpeti, anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ sāvasesā āpattīti dīpeti, duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.4
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi bhayāgatiṁ gacchanto bahujanāhitāya paṭipanno hoti bahujanāsukhāya bahuno janassa anatthāya ahitāya dukkhāya devamanussānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.5
Pali: Imehi aṭṭhārasahi vatthūhi bhayāgatiṁ gacchanto khataṁ upahataṁ attānaṁ pariharati, sāvajjo ca hoti, sānuvajjo ca viññūnaṁ, bahuñca apuññaṁ pasavati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:15.6
Pali: Bhayāgatiṁ gacchanto evaṁ bhayāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:16.1
Pali: Chandā dosā bhayā mohā, 

pli-tv-pvr15:16.2
Pali: yo dhammaṁ ativattati; 

pli-tv-pvr15:16.3
Pali: Nihīyati tassa yaso, 

pli-tv-pvr15:16.4
Pali: kāḷapakkheva candimāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:17.0
Pali: 3. Agatiagamana 

pli-tv-pvr15:17.1
Pali: Kathaṁ na chandāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:17.2
Pali: Adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, avinayaṁ avinayoti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, vinayaṁ vinayoti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatena abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatena bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, apaññattaṁ tathāgatena apaññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, paññattaṁ tathāgatena paññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, anāpattiṁ anāpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, āpattiṁ āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, lahukaṁ āpattiṁ lahukā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, garukaṁ āpattiṁ garukā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ sāvasesā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ anavasesā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na chandāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:17.3
Pali: Evaṁ na chandāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:18.1
Pali: Kathaṁ na dosāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:18.2
Pali: Adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpento na dosāgatiṁ gacchati, dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpento na dosāgatiṁ gacchati …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:18.3
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na dosāgatiṁ gacchati, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na dosāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:18.4
Pali: Evaṁ na dosāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:19.1
Pali: Kathaṁ na mohāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:19.2
Pali: Adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpento na mohāgatiṁ gacchati, dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpento na mohāgatiṁ gacchati …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:19.3
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na mohāgatiṁ gacchati, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na mohāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:19.4
Pali: Evaṁ na mohāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:20.1
Pali: Kathaṁ na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati? 

pli-tv-pvr15:20.2
Pali: Adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, avinayaṁ avinayoti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, vinayaṁ vinayoti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatena abhāsitaṁ alapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatena bhāsitaṁ lapitaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena anāciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatena āciṇṇaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, apaññattaṁ tathāgatena apaññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, paññattaṁ tathāgatena paññattaṁ tathāgatenāti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, anāpattiṁ anāpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, āpattiṁ āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, lahukaṁ āpattiṁ lahukā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, garukaṁ āpattiṁ garukā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, sāvasesaṁ āpattiṁ sāvasesā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, anavasesaṁ āpattiṁ anavasesā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati.

Pali: Evaṁ na bhayāgatiṁ gacchati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:21.1
Pali: Chandā dosā bhayā mohā, 

pli-tv-pvr15:21.2
Pali: yo dhammaṁ nātivattati; 

pli-tv-pvr15:21.3
Pali: Āpūrati tassa yaso, 

pli-tv-pvr15:21.4
Pali: sukkapakkheva candimāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:22.0
Pali: 4. Saññāpanīyādi

pli-tv-pvr15:23.4
Pali: Evaṁ nijjhāpanīye ṭhāne nijjhāpeti.

pli-tv-pvr15:24.2

Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento pekkhanīye ṭhāne pekkhati, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpento pekkhanīye ṭhāne pekkhati.

Pali: Evaṁ pekkhanīye ṭhāne pekkhati. 

pli-tv-pvr15:25.1

Pali: Adhammaṁ adhammoti dīpento pasādanīye ṭhāne pasādeti, dhammaṁ dhammoti dīpento pasādanīye ṭhāne pasādeti …pe…

pli-tv-pvr15:25.4
Pali: Evaṁ pasādanīye ṭhāne pasādeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.0
Pali: 5. Parapakkhādiavajānana 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.1
Pali: Kathaṁ laddhapakkhomhīti parapakkhaṁ avajānāti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.2
Pali: Idhekacco laddhapakkho hoti laddhaparivāro pakkhavā ñātimā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.3
Pali: “Ayaṁ aladdhapakkho aladdhaparivāro na pakkhavā na ñātimā”ti tassa avajānanto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.4
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:26.5
Pali: Evaṁ laddhapakkhomhīti parapakkhaṁ avajānāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:27.1
Pali: Kathaṁ bahussutomhīti appassutaṁ avajānāti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:27.2
Pali: Idhekacco bahussuto hoti sutadharo sutasannicayo. 

pli-tv-pvr15:27.3
Pali: “Ayaṁ appassuto appāgamo appadharo”ti tassa avajānanto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:27.4
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:27.5
Pali: Evaṁ bahussutomhīti appassutaṁ avajānāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:28.1
Pali: Kathaṁ therataromhīti navakataraṁ avajānāti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:28.2
Pali: Idhekacco thero hoti rattaññū cirapabbajito “ayaṁ navako appaññāto appakataññū imassa vacanaṁ akataṁ bhavissatī”ti tassa avajānanto adhammaṁ dhammoti dīpeti, dhammaṁ adhammoti dīpeti …pe… 

pli-tv-pvr15:28.3
Pali: duṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ aduṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti, aduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ duṭṭhullā āpattīti dīpeti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:28.4
Pali: Evaṁ therataromhīti navakataraṁ avajānāti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:29.1
Pali: Asampattaṁ na byāharitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:29.2
Pali: anotiṇṇaṁ bhāraṁ na otāretabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:29.3
Pali: Sampattaṁ dhammato vinayato na parihāpetabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:29.4
Pali: yaṁatthāya saṅgho sannipatito hoti, taṁ atthaṁ dhammato vinayato na parihāpetabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.1
Pali: Yena dhammenāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.2
Pali: bhūtena vatthunā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.3
Pali: Yena vinayenāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.4
Pali: codetvā sāretvā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.5
Pali: Yena satthusāsanenāti 

pli-tv-pvr15:30.6
Pali: ñattisampadāya anussāvanasampadāya, yena dhammena yena vinayena yena satthusāsanena taṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasammati, tathā taṁ adhikaraṇaṁ vūpasametabbanti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.0
Pali: 6. Anuvijjakassaanuyoga 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.1
Pali: Anuvijjakena codako pucchitabbo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.2
Pali: “yaṁ kho tvaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapesi, kimhi naṁ ṭhapesi, sīlavipattiyā vā ṭhapesi, ācāravipattiyā vā ṭhapesi, diṭṭhivipattiyā vā ṭhapesī”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.3
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.4
Pali: “sīlavipattiyā vā ṭhapemi, ācāravipattiyā vā ṭhapemi, diṭṭhivipattiyā vā ṭhapemī”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.5
Pali: “jānāti panāyasmā sīlavipattiṁ, jānāti ācāravipattiṁ, jānāti diṭṭhivipattin”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.6
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.7
Pali: “jānāmi kho ahaṁ, āvuso, sīlavipattiṁ, jānāmi ācāravipattiṁ, jānāmi diṭṭhivipattin”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.8
Pali: “katamā panāvuso, sīlavipatti, katamā ācāravipatti, katamā diṭṭhivipattī”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.9
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.10
Pali: “cattāri pārājikāni terasa saṅghādisesā—ayaṁ sīlavipatti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.11
Pali: Thullaccayaṁ pācittiyaṁ pāṭidesanīyaṁ dukkaṭaṁ dubbhāsitaṁ—ayaṁ ācāravipatti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.12
Pali: Micchādiṭṭhi antaggāhikādiṭṭhi—ayaṁ diṭṭhivipattī”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.13
Pali: “yaṁ kho tvaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapesi, diṭṭhena vā ṭhapesi, sutena vā ṭhapesi, parisaṅkāya vā ṭhapesī”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.14
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.15
Pali: “diṭṭhena vā ṭhapemi, sutena vā ṭhapemi, parisaṅkāya vā ṭhapemī”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.16
Pali: “yaṁ kho tvaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno diṭṭhena pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapesi, kiṁ te diṭṭhaṁ, kinti te diṭṭhaṁ, kadā te diṭṭhaṁ, kattha te diṭṭhaṁ, pārājikaṁ ajjhāpajjanto diṭṭho, saṅghādisesaṁ ajjhāpajjanto diṭṭho, thullaccayaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.17
Pali: pācittiyaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.18
Pali: pāṭidesanīyaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.19
Pali: dukkaṭaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.20
Pali: dubbhāsitaṁ ajjhāpajjanto diṭṭho, kattha ca tvaṁ ahosi, kattha cāyaṁ bhikkhu ahosi, kiñca tvaṁ karosi, kiṁ cāyaṁ bhikkhu karotī”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.21
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.22
Pali: “na kho ahaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno diṭṭhena pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapemi, api ca sutena pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapemī”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.23
Pali: “yaṁ kho tvaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno sutena pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapesi, kiṁ te sutaṁ, kinti te sutaṁ, kadā te sutaṁ, kattha te sutaṁ, pārājikaṁ ajjhāpannoti sutaṁ, saṅghādisesaṁ ajjhāpannoti sutaṁ, thullaccayaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.24
Pali: pācittiyaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.25
Pali: pāṭidesanīyaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.26
Pali: dukkaṭaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.27
Pali: dubbhāsitaṁ ajjhāpannoti sutaṁ, bhikkhussa sutaṁ, bhikkhuniyā sutaṁ, sikkhamānāya sutaṁ, sāmaṇerassa sutaṁ, sāmaṇeriyā sutaṁ, upāsakassa sutaṁ, upāsikāya sutaṁ, rājūnaṁ sutaṁ, rājamahāmattānaṁ sutaṁ, titthiyānaṁ sutaṁ, titthiyasāvakānaṁ sutan”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.28
Pali: So ce evaṁ vadeyya—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.29
Pali: “na kho ahaṁ, āvuso, imassa bhikkhuno sutena pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapemi, api ca parisaṅkāya pavāraṇaṁ ṭhapemī”ti, so evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr15:31.30

pli-tv-pvr15:31.32
Pali: pāṭidesanīyaṁ … 

pli-tv-pvr15:31.33

Pali: dubbhāsitaṁ ajjhāpannoti parisaṅkasi, bhikkhussa sutvā parisaṅkasi, bhikkhuniyā sutvā parisaṅkasi, sikkhamānāya sutvā parisaṅkasi, sāmaṇerassa sutvā parisaṅkasi, sāmaṇeriyā sutvā parisaṅkasi, upāsakassa sutvā parisaṅkasi, upāsikāya sutvā parisaṅkasi, rājūnaṁ sutvā parisaṅkasi, rājamahāmattānaṁ sutvā parisaṅkasi, titthiyānaṁ sutvā parisaṅkasi, titthiyasāvakānaṁ sutvā parisaṅkasī”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.1
Pali: Diṭṭhaṁ diṭṭhena sameti, 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.2
Pali: diṭṭhena saṁsandate diṭṭhaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.3
Pali: Diṭṭhaṁ paṭicca na upeti, 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.4
Pali: asuddhaparisaṅkito; 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.5
Pali: So puggalo paṭiññāya, 

pli-tv-pvr15:32.6
Pali: kātabbā tena pavāraṇā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:33.1
Pali: Sutaṁ sutena sameti, 

pli-tv-pvr15:33.2
Pali: sutena saṁsandate sutaṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr15:33.3
Pali: Sutaṁ paṭicca na upeti,

pli-tv-pvr15:35.0
Pali: 7. Pucchāvibhāga 

pli-tv-pvr15:35.1
Pali: Kiṁ te diṭṭhanti katamā pucchā? 

pli-tv-pvr15:35.2
Pali: Kinti te diṭṭhanti katamā pucchā? 

pli-tv-pvr15:35.3
Pali: Kadā te diṭṭhanti katamā pucchā? 

pli-tv-pvr15:35.4
Pali: Kattha te diṭṭhanti katamā pucchā? 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.1
Pali: Kiṁ te diṭṭhanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.2
Pali: vatthupucchā, vipattipucchā, āpattipucchā, ajjhācārapucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.3
Pali: Vatthupucchāti—

pli-tv-pvr15:36.4
Pali: aṭṭhapārājikānaṁ vatthupucchā, tevīsasaṅghādisesānaṁ vatthupucchā, dveaniyatānaṁ vatthupucchā, dvecattārīsanissaggiyānaṁ vatthupucchā, aṭṭhāsītisatapācittiyānaṁ vatthupucchā, dvādasapāṭidesanīyānaṁ vatthupucchā, dukkaṭānaṁ vatthupucchā, dubbhāsitānaṁ vatthupucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.5
Pali: Vipattipucchāti—

pli-tv-pvr15:36.6
Pali: sīlavipattipucchā, ācāravipattipucchā, diṭṭhivipattipucchā, ājīvavipattipucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.7
Pali: Āpattipucchāti—

pli-tv-pvr15:36.8
Pali: pārājikāpattipucchā, saṅghādisesāpattipucchā, thullaccayāpattipucchā, pācittiyāpattipucchā, pāṭidesanīyāpattipucchā, dukkaṭāpattipucchā, dubbhāsitāpattipucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:36.9
Pali: Ajjhācārapucchāti—

pli-tv-pvr15:36.10
Pali: dvayaṁdvayasamāpattipucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.1
Pali: Kinti te diṭṭhanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.2
Pali: liṅgapucchā, iriyāpathapucchā, ākārapucchā, vippakārapucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.3
Pali: Liṅgapucchāti—dīghaṁ vā rassaṁ vā kaṇhaṁ vā odātaṁ vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.4
Pali: Iriyāpathapucchāti gacchantaṁ vā ṭhitaṁ vā nisinnaṁ vā nipannaṁ vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.5
Pali: Ākārapucchāti gihiliṅge vā titthiyaliṅge vā pabbajitaliṅge vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:37.6
Pali: Vippakārapucchāti gacchantaṁ vā ṭhitaṁ vā nisinnaṁ vā nipannaṁ vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.1
Pali: Kadā te diṭṭhanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.2
Pali: kālapucchā, samayapucchā, divasapucchā, utupucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.3
Pali: Kālapucchāti pubbaṇhakāle vā majjhanhikakāle vā sāyanhakāle vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.4
Pali: Samayapucchāti pubbaṇhasamaye vā majjhanhikasamaye vā sāyanhasamaye vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.5
Pali: Divasapucchāti purebhattaṁ vā pacchābhattaṁ vā rattiṁ vā divā vā kāḷe vā juṇhe vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:38.6
Pali: Utupucchāti hemante vā gimhe vā vasse vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.1
Pali: Kattha te diṭṭhanti 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.2
Pali: ṭhānapucchā, bhūmipucchā, okāsapucchā, padesapucchā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.3
Pali: Ṭhānapucchāti bhūmiyā vā pathaviyā vā dharaṇiyā vā jagatiyā vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.4
Pali: Bhūmipucchāti bhūmiyā vā pathaviyā vā pabbate vā pāsāṇe vā pāsāde vā. 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.5
Pali: Okāsapucchāti puratthime vā okāse pacchime vā okāse uttare vā okāse dakkhiṇe vā okāse. 

pli-tv-pvr15:39.6
Pali: Padesapucchāti puratthime vā padese pacchime vā padese uttare vā padese dakkhiṇe vā padeseti. 

pli-tv-pvr15:40.1
Pali: Mahāsaṅgāmaṁ niṭṭhitaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr15:41.1
Pali: Tassuddānaṁ 

pli-tv-pvr15:42.1
Pali: Vatthu nidānaṁ ākāro, 

pli-tv-pvr15:42.2
Pali: pubbāparaṁ katākataṁ; 

pli-tv-pvr15:42.3
Pali: Kammādhikaraṇañceva, 

pli-tv-pvr15:42.4
Pali: samatho chandagāmi ca. 

pli-tv-pvr15:43.1
Pali: Dosā mohā bhayā ceva, 

pli-tv-pvr15:43.2
Pali: saññā nijjhāpanena ca; 

pli-tv-pvr15:43.3
Pali: Pekkhā pasāde pakkhomhi, 

pli-tv-pvr15:43.4
Pali: sutatheratarena ca. 

pli-tv-pvr15:44.1
Pali: Asampattañca sampattaṁ, 

pli-tv-pvr15:44.2
Pali: dhammena vinayena ca; 

pli-tv-pvr15:44.3
Pali: Satthussa sāsanenāpi, 

pli-tv-pvr15:44.4
Pali: mahāsaṅgāmañāpanāti.

Pali: Pannarasa dhammā sahajātapaccayena paccayo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:9.21
Pali: Āsā ca anāsā ca vatthussa anantarapaccayena paccayo, samanantarapaccayena paccayo, nissayapaccayena paccayo, upanissayapaccayena paccayo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:9.22
Pali: Vatthu āsānañca anāsānañca purejātapaccayena paccayo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:9.23
Pali: Āsā ca anāsā ca vatthussa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:9.24
Pali: Pannarasa dhammā sahajātapaccayena paccayo.

pli-tv-pvr16:10.1

pli-tv-pvr16:11.1

pli-tv-pvr16:16.1
Pali: Pubbakaraṇaṁ katihi dhammehi saṅgahitaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:16.2
Pali: Pubbakaraṇaṁ sattahi dhammehi saṅgahitaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:16.3
Pali: Dhovanena, vicāraṇena, chedanena, bandhanena, sibbanena, rajanena, kappakaraṇena—

pli-tv-pvr16:16.4
Pali: pubbakaraṇaṁ imehi sattahi dhammehi saṅgahitaṁ.

Pali: Paccuddhāro katihi dhammehi saṅgahito? 

pli-tv-pvr16:17.2

pli-tv-pvr16:17.3
Pali: saṅghāṭiyā, uttarāsaṅgena, antaravāsakena. 

pli-tv-pvr16:18.1
Pali: Adhiṭṭhānaṁ katihi dhammehi saṅgahitaṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:18.2
Pali: Adhiṭṭhānaṁ tīhi dhammehi saṅgahitaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr16:18.3
Pali: saṅghāṭiyā, uttarāsaṅgena, antaravāsakena. 

pli-tv-pvr16:19.1
Pali: Atthāro katihi dhammehi saṅgahito? 

pli-tv-pvr16:19.2
Pali: Atthāro ekena dhammena saṅgahito—

pli-tv-pvr16:19.3
Pali: vacībhedena. 

pli-tv-pvr16:20.1
Pali: Kathinassa kati mūlāni, kati vatthūni, kati bhūmiyo? 

pli-tv-pvr16:20.2
Pali: Kathinassa ekaṁ mūlaṁ—

pli-tv-pvr16:20.3
Pali: saṅgho; 

pli-tv-pvr16:20.4
Pali: tīṇi vatthūni—

pli-tv-pvr16:20.5
Pali: saṅghāṭi, uttarāsaṅgo, antaravāsako; 

pli-tv-pvr16:20.6
Pali: cha bhūmiyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:20.7
Pali: khomaṁ, kappāsikaṁ, koseyyaṁ, kambalaṁ, sāṇaṁ, bhaṅgaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr16:21.2
Pali: Kathinassa pubbakaraṇaṁ ādi, kriyā majjhe, atthāro pariyosānaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.1
Pali: Katihaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo abhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.2
Pali: Katihaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo bhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.3
Pali: Aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo abhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.4
Pali: Aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo bhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.5
Pali: Katamehi aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo abhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.6
Pali: Pubbakaraṇaṁ na jānāti, paccuddhāraṁ na jānāti, adhiṭṭhānaṁ na jānāti, atthāraṁ na jānāti, mātikaṁ na jānāti, palibodhaṁ na jānāti, uddhāraṁ na jānāti, ānisaṁsaṁ na jānāti—

pli-tv-pvr16:22.7
Pali: imehi aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo abhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.8
Pali: Katamehi aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo bhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ? 

pli-tv-pvr16:22.9
Pali: Pubbakaraṇaṁ jānāti, paccuddhāraṁ jānāti, adhiṭṭhānaṁ jānāti, atthāraṁ jānāti, mātikaṁ jānāti, palibodhaṁ jānāti, uddhāraṁ jānāti, ānisaṁsaṁ jānāti—

pli-tv-pvr16:22.10
Pali: imehi aṭṭhahaṅgehi samannāgato puggalo bhabbo kathinaṁ attharituṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.1
Pali: Katinaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā na ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.2
Pali: Katinaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.3
Pali: Tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā na ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.4
Pali: Tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.5
Pali: Katamesaṁ tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā na ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.6
Pali: Nissīmaṭṭho anumodati, anumodento na vācaṁ bhindati, vācaṁ bhindanto na paraṁ viññāpeti—

pli-tv-pvr16:23.7
Pali: imesaṁ tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā na ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.8
Pali: Katamesaṁ tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:23.9
Pali: Sīmaṭṭho anumodati, anumodento vācaṁ bhindati, vācaṁ bhindanto paraṁ viññāpeti—

pli-tv-pvr16:23.10
Pali: imesaṁ tiṇṇaṁ puggalānaṁ kathinatthārā ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.1
Pali: Kati kathinatthārā na ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.2
Pali: Kati kathinatthārā ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.3
Pali: Tayo kathinatthārā na ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.4
Pali: Tayo kathinatthārā ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.5
Pali: Katame tayo kathinatthārā na ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.6
Pali: Vatthuvipannañceva hoti, kālavipannañca, karaṇavipannañca—

pli-tv-pvr16:24.7
Pali: ime tayo kathinatthārā na ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.8
Pali: Katame tayo kathinatthārā ruhanti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:24.9
Pali: Vatthusampannañceva hoti, kālasampannañca, karaṇasampannañca—

pli-tv-pvr16:24.10
Pali: ime tayo kathinatthārā ruhanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:25.0
Pali: 4. Kathinādijānitabbavibhāga 

pli-tv-pvr16:25.1
Pali: Kathinaṁ jānitabbaṁ, kathinatthāro jānitabbo, kathinassa atthāramāso jānitabbo, kathinassa atthāravipatti jānitabbā, kathinassa atthārasampatti jānitabbā, nimittakammaṁ jānitabbaṁ, parikathā jānitabbā, kukkukataṁ jānitabbaṁ, sannidhi jānitabbā, nissaggiyaṁ jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:26.1
Pali: Kathinaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr16:26.2
Pali: tesaññeva dhammānaṁ saṅgaho samavāyo nāmaṁ nāmakammaṁ nāmadheyyaṁ nirutti byañjanaṁ abhilāpo yadidaṁ kathinanti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:27.1
Pali: Kathinassa atthāramāso jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr16:27.2
Pali: vassānassa pacchimo māso jānitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:28.1
Pali: Kathinassa atthāravipatti jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr16:28.2
Pali: catuvīsatiyā ākārehi kathinassa atthāravipatti jānitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:29.1
Pali: Kathinassa atthārasampatti jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr16:29.2
Pali: sattarasahi ākārehi kathinassa atthārasampatti jānitabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:30.1
Pali: Nimittakammaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr16:30.2
Pali: nimittaṁ karoti iminā dussena kathinaṁ attharissāmīti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:31.1
Pali: Parikathā jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr16:31.2
Pali: parikathaṁ karoti imāya parikathāya kathinadussaṁ nibbattessāmīti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:32.1
Pali: Kukkukataṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr16:32.2
Pali: anādiyadānaṁ jānitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:33.1
Pali: Sannidhi jānitabbāti 

pli-tv-pvr16:33.2
Pali: dve sannidhiyo jānitabbā—karaṇasannidhi vā nicayasannidhi vā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:34.1
Pali: Nissaggiyaṁ jānitabbanti 

pli-tv-pvr16:34.2
Pali: kariyamāne aruṇaṁ uṭṭhahati. 

pli-tv-pvr16:35.1
Pali: Kathinatthāro jānitabboti 

pli-tv-pvr16:35.2
Pali: sace saṅghassa kathinadussaṁ uppannaṁ hoti, saṅghena kathaṁ paṭipajjitabbaṁ, atthārakena kathaṁ paṭipajjitabbaṁ, anumodakena kathaṁ paṭipajjitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.1
Pali: Saṅghena ñattidutiyena kammena kathinatthārakassa bhikkhuno dātabbaṁ, tena kathinatthārakena bhikkhunā tadaheva dhovitvā vimajjitvā vicāretvā chinditvā sibbetvā rajitvā kappaṁ katvā kathinaṁ attharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.2
Pali: Sace saṅghāṭiyā kathinaṁ attharitukāmo hoti, porāṇikā saṅghāṭi paccuddharitabbā, navā saṅghāṭi adhiṭṭhātabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.3
Pali: Imāya saṅghāṭiyā kathinaṁ attharāmīti vācā bhinditabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.4
Pali: Sace uttarāsaṅgena kathinaṁ attharitukāmo hoti, porāṇako uttarāsaṅgo paccuddharitabbo, navo uttarāsaṅgo adhiṭṭhātabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.5
Pali: Iminā uttarāsaṅgena kathinaṁ attharāmīti vācā bhinditabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.6
Pali: Sace antaravāsakena kathinaṁ attharitukāmo hoti, porāṇako antaravāsako paccuddharitabbo, navo antaravāsako adhiṭṭhātabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.7
Pali: Iminā antaravāsakena kathinaṁ attharāmīti vācā bhinditabbā. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.8
Pali: Tena kathinatthārakena bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.9
Pali: “atthataṁ, bhante, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro, anumodathā”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.10
Pali: Tehi anumodakehi bhikkhūhi ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.11
Pali: “atthataṁ, āvuso, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro, anumodāmā”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.12
Pali: Tena kathinatthārakena bhikkhunā sambahule bhikkhū upasaṅkamitvā ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassu vacanīyā—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.13
Pali: “atthataṁ, bhante, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro, anumodathā”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.14
Pali: Tehi anumodakehi bhikkhūhi ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.15
Pali: “atthataṁ, āvuso, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro anumodāmā”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.16
Pali: Tena kathinatthārakena bhikkhunā ekaṁ bhikkhuṁ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.17
Pali: “atthataṁ, āvuso, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro, anumodāhī”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:36.18
Pali: Tena anumodakena bhikkhunā ekaṁsaṁ uttarāsaṅgaṁ karitvā añjaliṁ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo—

pli-tv-pvr16:36.19
Pali: “atthataṁ, āvuso, saṅghassa kathinaṁ, dhammiko kathinatthāro, anumodāmī”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.0
Pali: 5. Puggalassevakathinatthāra 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.1
Pali: Saṅgho kathinaṁ attharati, gaṇo kathinaṁ attharati, puggalo kathinaṁ attharatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.2
Pali: Na saṅgho kathinaṁ attharati, na gaṇo kathinaṁ attharati, puggalo kathinaṁ attharatīti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.3
Pali: Hañci na saṅgho kathinaṁ attharati, na gaṇo kathinaṁ attharati, puggalo kathinaṁ attharati. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.4
Pali: Saṅghassa anatthataṁ hoti kathinaṁ, gaṇassa anatthataṁ hoti kathinaṁ, puggalassa atthataṁ hoti kathinaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.5
Pali: Saṅgho pātimokkhaṁ uddisati gaṇo pātimokkhaṁ uddisati puggalo pātimokkhaṁ uddisatīti? 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.6
Pali: Na saṅgho pātimokkhaṁ uddisati, na gaṇo pātimokkhaṁ uddisati, puggalo pātimokkhaṁ uddisatīti. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.7
Pali: Hañci na saṅgho pātimokkhaṁ uddisati, na gaṇo pātimokkhaṁ uddisati, puggalo pātimokkhaṁ uddisati. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.8
Pali: Saṅghassa anuddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ, gaṇassa anuddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ, puggalassa uddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.9
Pali: Saṅghassa sāmaggiyā gaṇassa sāmaggiyā puggalassa uddesā saṅghassa uddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ, gaṇassa uddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ, puggalassa uddiṭṭhaṁ hoti pātimokkhaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.10
Pali: Evameva na saṅgho kathinaṁ attharati, na gaṇo kathinaṁ attharati, puggalo kathinaṁ attharati. 

pli-tv-pvr16:37.11
Pali: Saṅghassa anumodanāya gaṇassa anumodanāya puggalassa atthārā saṅghassa atthataṁ hoti kathinaṁ, gaṇassa atthataṁ hoti kathinaṁ, puggalassa atthataṁ hoti kathinanti.

Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:11.3

pli-tv-pvr17:11.4

pli-tv-pvr17:16.3

pli-tv-pvr17:17.4

pli-tv-pvr17:21.3
Pali: Yāyāpattiyā buddhassa, 

pli-tv-pvr17:21.4
Pali: paṭhamo vaggasaṅgahoti. 

pli-tv-pvr17:22.0

pli-tv-pvr17:23.1
Pali: “Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ nappaṭippassambhetabbaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr17:24.4

Pali: Buddhassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsati, dhammassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsati, saṅghassa avaṇṇaṁ bhāsati, micchādiṭṭhiko ca hoti, ājīvavipanno ca—

pli-tv-pvr17:25.4

pli-tv-pvr17:26.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:26.3
Pali: Alajjī ca hoti, bālo ca, apakatatto ca, omaddakārako ca hoti, vattesu sikkhāya ca na paripūrakārī—

pli-tv-pvr17:26.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatassa bhikkhuno kammaṁ nappaṭippassambhetabban”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr17:27.1
Pali: “Saṅgāmāvacarena, bhante, bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamantena kati dhamme ajjhattaṁ upaṭṭhāpetvā saṅgho upasaṅkamitabbo”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.1
Pali: “Saṅgāmāvacarena, upāli, bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamantena pañca dhamme ajjhattaṁ upaṭṭhāpetvā saṅgho upasaṅkamitabbo. 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.2
Pali: Katame pañca? 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.3
Pali: Saṅgāmāvacarena, upāli, bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamantena nīcacittena saṅgho upasaṅkamitabbo, rajoharaṇasamena cittena, āsanakusalena bhavitabbaṁ nissajjakusalena, there bhikkhū anupakhajjantena, nave bhikkhū āsanena appaṭibāhantena yathāpatirūpe āsane nisīditabbaṁ, anānākathikena bhavitabbaṁ atiracchānakathikena, sāmaṁ vā dhammo bhāsitabbo, paro vā ajjhesitabbo, ariyo vā tuṇhībhāvo nātimaññitabbo, sace, upāli, saṅgho samaggakaraṇīyāni kammāni karoti; 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.4
Pali: tatra ce, upāli, bhikkhuno nakkhamati, api diṭṭhāvikammaṁ katvā ñāpetabbā sāmaggī. 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.5
Pali: Taṁ kissahetu? 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.6
Pali: Māhaṁ saṅghena nānatto assanti. 

pli-tv-pvr17:28.7
Pali: Saṅgāmāvacarenupāli, bhikkhunā saṅghaṁ upasaṅkamantena ime pañca dhamme ajjhattaṁ upaṭṭhāpetvā saṅgho upasaṅkamitabbo”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr17:29.1
Pali: “Katihi nu kho, bhante, aṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanaakanto ca hoti bahujanaamanāpo ca bahujanaarucito cā”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr17:30.1

pli-tv-pvr17:30.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:30.3
Pali: Ussitamantī ca hoti, nissitajappī ca, na ca bhāsānusandhikusalo hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:30.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanaakanto ca hoti bahujanaamanāpo ca bahujanaarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:30.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:30.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:30.7
Pali: Na ussitamantī ca hoti, na nissitajappī ca, bhāsānusandhikusalo ca hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:30.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.1
Pali: Aparehipi, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanaakanto ca hoti bahujanaamanāpo ca bahujanaarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.3

pli-tv-pvr17:31.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanaakanto ca hoti bahujanaamanāpo ca bahujanaarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:31.7
Pali: Na ussādetā ca hoti, na apasādetā ca, dhammaṁ gaṇhāti, adhammaṁ paṭibāhati, samphañca na bahuṁ bhāsati—

pli-tv-pvr17:31.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:32.1
Pali: Aparehipi, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanaakanto ca hoti bahujanaamanāpo ca bahujanaarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:32.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:32.3
Pali: Pasayhapavattā hoti, anokāsakammaṁ kāretvā pavattā hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti, na yathādiṭṭhiyā byākatā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:32.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito ca. 

pli-tv-pvr17:32.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:32.7
Pali: Na pasayhapavattā hoti, okāsakammaṁ kāretvā pavattā hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti, yathādiṭṭhiyā byākatā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:32.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato bhikkhu saṅghe voharanto bahujanakanto ca hoti bahujanamanāpo ca bahujanarucito cā”ti. 

pli-tv-pvr17:33.1
Pali: “Kati nu kho, bhante, ānisaṁsā vinayapariyattiyā”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr17:34.1

Pali: Katame pañca? 

pli-tv-pvr17:34.3
Pali: Attano sīlakkhandho sugutto hoti surakkhito, kukkuccapakatānaṁ paṭisaraṇaṁ hoti, visārado saṅghamajjhe voharati, paccatthike sahadhammena suniggahitaṁ niggaṇhāti, saddhammaṭṭhitiyā paṭipanno hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:34.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcānisaṁsā vinayapariyattiyā”.

Pali: Nappaṭippassambhanavaggo niṭṭhito dutiyo.

pli-tv-pvr17:37.4
Pali: pasayha pariyattiyāti.

pli-tv-pvr17:39.0
Pali: 3. Vohāravagga 

pli-tv-pvr17:39.1
Pali: “Katihi nu kho, bhante, aṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabban”ti 

pli-tv-pvr17:40.1
Pali: “Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ.

Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:40.3

pli-tv-pvr17:40.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:40.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:40.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:40.7
Pali: Āpattiṁ jānāti, āpattisamuṭṭhānaṁ jānāti, āpattiyā payogaṁ jānāti, āpattiyā vūpasamaṁ jānāti, āpattiyā vinicchayakusalo hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:40.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ.

pli-tv-pvr17:41.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:41.5

pli-tv-pvr17:41.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:41.7
Pali: Adhikaraṇaṁ jānāti, adhikaraṇasamuṭṭhānaṁ jānāti, adhikaraṇassa payogaṁ jānāti, adhikaraṇassa vūpasamaṁ jānāti, adhikaraṇassa vinicchayakusalo hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:41.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ.

Pali: Aparehipi, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:42.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:42.3
Pali: Pasayhapavattā hoti, anokāsakammaṁ kāretvā pavattā hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, na yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti, na yathādiṭṭhiyā byākatā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:42.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:42.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:42.6
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:42.7
Pali: Na pasayhapavattā hoti, okāsakammaṁ kāretvā pavattā hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā codetā hoti, yathādhamme yathāvinaye yathāpattiyā kāretā hoti, yathādiṭṭhiyā byākatā hoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:42.8
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:43.1
Pali: Aparehipi, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:43.2
Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:43.3
Pali: Āpattānāpattiṁ na jānāti, lahukagarukaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, sāvasesānavasesaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, duṭṭhullāduṭṭhullaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti, sappaṭikammaṁ appaṭikammaṁ āpattiṁ na jānāti—

pli-tv-pvr17:43.4
Pali: imehi kho, upāli, pañcahaṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe na voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:43.5
Pali: Pañcahupāli, aṅgehi samannāgatena bhikkhunā saṅghe voharitabbaṁ. 

pli-tv-pvr17:43.6

pli-tv-pvr17:54.0
Pali: 4. Diṭṭhāvikammavagga 

pli-tv-pvr17:54.1
Pali: “Kati nu kho, bhante, adhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā”ti? 

pli-tv-pvr17:55.1
Pali: “Pañcime, upāli, adhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā. 

pli-tv-pvr17:55.2
Pali: Katame pañca? 

pli-tv-pvr17:55.3
Pali: Anāpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, adesanāgāminiyā āpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, desitāya āpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, catūhi pañcahi diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, mano mānasena diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:55.4
Pali: ime kho, upāli, pañca adhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā. 

pli-tv-pvr17:56.1
Pali: Pañcime, upāli, dhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā. 

pli-tv-pvr17:56.2
Pali: Katame pañca? 

pli-tv-pvr17:56.3
Pali: Āpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, desanāgāminiyā āpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, adesitāya āpattiyā diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, na catūhi pañcahi diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, na mano mānasena diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti—

pli-tv-pvr17:56.4
Pali: ime kho, upāli, pañca dhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā. 

pli-tv-pvr17:57.1
Pali: Aparepi, upāli, pañca adhammikā diṭṭhāvikammā. 

pli-tv-pvr17:57.2
Pali: Katame pañca? 

pli-tv-pvr17:57.3
Pali: Nānāsaṁvāsakassa santike diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, nānāsīmāya ṭhitassa santike diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, apakatattassa santike diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, catūhi pañcahi diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti, mano mānasena diṭṭhiṁ āvi karoti—

Pali: Katamehi pañcahi? 

pli-tv-pvr17:72.3
